# Disclaimer | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/welcome-to-the-guide/disclaimer.md)
.

_This git book is not affiliated in any way with the 7thBeat Games Team or their games_

_All pages are based on and updated up to version 2.5.0 (windows) of the game editor (currently updating it). Some of the videos and images used can include old versions of the editor's UI and other visuals, this content will be updated when needed._

_Anything that indicates the emoji_ 📝_comes from an external source. We do not own this content; we merely address it for informative purposes, while crediting the same who wrote and created it._

_This git book documentation is under_ [**CC BY-NC-ND 4.0** **International**](https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by-nc-nd/4.0/)
 _license._

# How to use & search the Guide | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/welcome-to-the-guide/how-to-use-and-search-the-guide.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/welcome-to-the-guide/how-to-use-and-search-the-guide#color-and-index-format)

• **Color and Index Format:**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

_**Here are some pointers to help you learn more efficiently**_

**Bold - Keywords**

_Italic - Additional information_

Blue - Links

Purple - Editor Guide Pages

Orange - In-game Sections

Yellow - Keyboard Shortcuts

Red - Negative Feedback

Green - Positive Feedback

* * *

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/welcome-to-the-guide/how-to-use-and-search-the-guide#using-the-search-bar-detailed-search)

• Using the search bar (Detailed search)


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For detailed results with specific terms, use the search bar at the top right of this guide website.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FudCi64tRlNieG7Q3thpM%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D75dfa25f-0ef1-4f86-9d72-3698aaf04418&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d2de964a&sv=2)

Editor Guide - Using the search bar

Access the **search menu** at any time by pressing the `Ctrl``+``K` shortcut.

When you add your topics, the guide will search for both **page names** and **keywords** within each topic to find all results according to your search.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FTFfRVOz36zACwmzSdlFA%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D41d50a00-2b36-4aab-8d2b-cba85e308d82&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8077e698&sv=2)

Editor Guide - Search Results (Red: Page name ~ Orange: Keyword)

Choose the best option to quickly navigate directly to that page!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FBRlXUEbYXmXXtKITuYKC%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D062b59f4-01c4-40e1-99e5-f8d9d9dd28c5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9894b1b5&sv=2)

Editor Guide - Searched Page

* * *

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/welcome-to-the-guide/how-to-use-and-search-the-guide#using-the-directory-left-tab-step-by-step-search)

• Using the Directory / Left Tab (Step by Step search)


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For searches where you're unsure of what to look for, but have a general idea of your goal, it's beneficial to explore step by step. Navigate through information to find your golden nugget of knowledge.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F62YlqTLj18YRg8Ixu1YM%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D304e7a9b-0ba8-4d2a-8018-a62d45886b0c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4ec0ea9a&sv=2)

Editor Guide - Directory (Red: Left Page List ~ Green: Page Linking ~ Yellow: Search bar)

Each main topic page includes illustrative page link cards that help visualize content related to each subtopic found within the pages.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fmk1jidhOcQW7zDap8tju%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7ac2ea34-51a5-4695-a0a5-8da942179727&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=395f51ca&sv=2)

Editor Guide - Step by Step search (Red: Head Page ~ Green: Sub Page)

Finally, as you research everything necessary for your upcoming Top Level creation, persistently apply this method until you reach your desired topic!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F85NIGKGZRD6HugvuLt8D%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df4b0ae68-1c13-4cad-8644-705b9207dec5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=16a05150&sv=2)

Editor Guide - Step by Step final search

\[Events\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events.md): Here you can find a complex description of all the editor events and how to use them correctly and the most efficient - \[Gameplay Events\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events.md): From the Events page - \[Set Speed\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events/set-speed.md): Sets the speed (BPM) - \[Twirl\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events/twirl.md): Changes the planets rotation - \[Checkpoint\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events/checkpoint.md): Saves player's progress, returning to this point in case of losing - \[Set Hitsound\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events/set-hitsound.md): Defines the sound for each following hit - \[Play Sound\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events/play-sound.md): Plays a hitsound regardless the current hitsound (one time event) - \[Set Planet Orbit\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events/set-planet-orbit.md): Changes the way how both planets rotate around each other - \[Pause Tiles\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events/pause-tiles.md): Pauses the path gameplay for a certain number of beats - \[AutoPlay Tiles\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events/autoplay-tiles.md): Plays the following path automatically, without any player input necessary - \[Scale Planets\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events/scale-planets.md): Scales the desired planet to a different size (does not influence rotation scale) - \[Track Events\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/track-events.md): From the Events page - \[Set Track Color\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/track-events/set-track-color.md): Track color distribution, from tile to tile up to color fusion like rainbows - \[Set Track Animation\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/track-events/set-track-animation.md): Animation section that makes tiles appear and disappear on the track and how long ahead/behind - \[Recolor Track\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/track-events/recolor-track.md): Track recolor when activated. Works on the distribution, color and glow intensity during gameplay - \[Move Track\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/track-events/move-track.md): Track reposition when activated. Works on the size, placement, rotation and tile opacity during gameplay - \[Position Track\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/track-events/position-track.md): Track set position. Works on the size, placement, rotation and tile opacity prior to gameplay, its stays indepedent until changes occur - \[Decoration Events\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/decoration-events.md): From the Events page - \[Move Decorations\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/decoration-events/move-decorations.md): Set specific actions such as change position, rotation, opacity, color, depth, masks and others for decorations - \[Set Text\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/decoration-events/set-text.md): Transform current Text lines into new text - \[Emit Particle\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/decoration-events/emit-particle.md): Coming Soon (Work In Progress Page) - \[Set Particle\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/decoration-events/set-particle.md): Coming Soon (Work In Progress Page) - \[Set Object\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/decoration-events/set-object.md): Coming Soon (Work In Progress Page) - \[Set Default Text\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/decoration-events/set-default-text.md): Coming Soon (Work In Progress Page) - \[Visual Effects\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects.md): From the Events page - \[Set Background\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/set-background.md): Insert/replace new background - \[Flash\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/flash.md): Creates a flash lighting over the background or its entire level area - \[Move Camera\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/move-camera.md): Move the position, rotation, zoom or target POV of the camera - \[Set Filter\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/set-filter.md): Enable/Disable filters and its duration - \[Set Filter Advanced\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/set-filter-advanced.md): Coming Soon (Work in Progress Page) - \[Hall Of Mirrors\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/hall-of-mirrors.md): Creates an illusion effect of delayed frames on top of each other - \[Shake Screen\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/shake-screen.md): Shakes the screen for a certain amount of beats, adjusting its shake strength and speed - \[Bloom\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/bloom.md): Creates a bloom ligthing effect for the entire level, adjusting its intesity and color - \[Tile Screen\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/tile-screen.md): Splits the screen into several smaller screens of equal size - \[Scroll Screen\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/scroll-screen.md): Moves the current screen at a certain speed causing the camera area to loop around itself - \[Set Frame Rate\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/set-frame-rate.md): Coming Soon (Work in Progress Page) - \[Event Modifiers\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/event-modifiers.md): From the Events page - \[Repeat Events\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/event-modifiers/repeat-events.md): Creates a repetition event to repeat several tasks for a number of times, during a certain time - \[Set Conditional Events\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/event-modifiers/set-conditional-events.md): Creates an event that causes specified events to occur when a certain gameplay condition occurs - \[Set Input Event\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/event-modifiers/set-input-event.md): Coming Soon (Work In Progress Page) - \[Conveniences\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/conveniences.md): From the Events page - \[Editor Comment\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/conveniences/editor-comment.md): A commentary section, for the editor side, to storage important information of a specific tile functionality or thought process. (Works with HTML format) - \[Bookmark\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/conveniences/bookmark.md): Save important locations on your level map, for the editor side, and fast travel to them using its shortcut triggers - \[DLC Events\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/dlc-events.md): From the Events page - \[Hold\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/dlc-events/hold.md): Forces the player to hold the key until the hold ends to proceed on the level rather than single tapping the tile - \[Set Hold Sound\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/dlc-events/set-hold-sound.md): Sound that will play while doing the Hold event - \[Multi Planet\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/dlc-events/multi-planet.md): Transforms the player into 2 or 3 planets - \[Freeroam Segment\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/dlc-events/freeroam-segment.md): Section where rhythm play isn't the main force, this section creates an open area of tiles where the player can travel freely around with no risk of faling to the beat - \[Freeroam Twirl\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/dlc-events/freeroam-twirl.md): Changes the planets rotation, exclusive to the freeroam section area - \[Freeroam Remove\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/dlc-events/freeroam-remove.md): Create off to reach areas inside the freeroam area segment - \[Hide Judgement / Floor Icons\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/dlc-events/hide-judgement-floor-icons.md): Hides/Shows all gameplay info and tile icons - \[Timing Window Scale\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/dlc-events/timing-window-scale.md): Reduces/Increases the gameplay error window from the player - \[Planet Radius Scale\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/dlc-events/planet-radius-scale.md): Reduces/Increases the planet center radius - \[Favorites\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/favorites.md): Add and remove events of your choice to turn your editor experience more practically - \[Level Preparation and Assisting Techniques\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques.md): Only pros can know how to be the coolest - \[Good Practices\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices.md): Better learn first and make mistakes later imo - \[BPM Speeds\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/bpm-speeds.md): From Good Practices - \[Under / Over Charting\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/under-over-charting.md): It's good to know when it's not enough, or when you're exaggerating. - \[Hidden Twirls and On-beat rotation\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/hidden-twirls-and-on-beat-rotation.md): From Good Practices - \[Smooth Pauses\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/smooth-pauses.md): From Good Practices - \[Formatting Styles\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/formatting-styles.md): Bring some customization to your text notes and titles - \[Difficulty Scoring Methods\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/difficulty-scoring-methods.md): A suggestive method to help decide how difficult your level is scored - ###

# Level Settings | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/level-settings.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/level-settings#list-of-settings)

List of Settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setting Name

Type Validation

Description

Artist

Text

Name of the composer

Special Artist Type

Multiple Selection

Description of the license from the Music of said Artist

Proof of artist's permission

File

Image or document proving the Artist allows the usage of their music

Song

Text

Name of the music

Author

Text

Name of the Level creator

Portal Image

Image File

Image for the portal display at the custom levels list

Level Icon

Image File

Image for the tile icon at the custom levels list

Level Icon Color

Hex Code

Color range value for the icon image

Song Preview Start

Numerical

The start point, in seconds, of the music during Custom Level selection

Song Preview Duration

Numerical

How long, in seconds, the music plays when on the Custom Level selection

Seizure Warning

Radio Selection

Indicate if your level can cause any issues to people with Epilepsy

Level Description

Text

Description for your level theme and gameplay style. Can be also used as a level introduction or crediting

Level Tags

Text

Single word indicators to find your level. Separate each tag with commas

Artist links

Text

URL info about the artist. Separate each URL with commas

Speed Trial Multiplier Aim

Numerical

Sets the speed trial goal to your level

Difficulty

Multiple Selection

1 to 10 scoring on level difficulty

In case the music has a **public license**, or you are the artist, permission is **not required** on Proof of Artist's Permission

For better knowledge on how to **score the difficulty** of your level, go to [Difficulty Scoring Methods](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/difficulty-scoring-methods)

To fully customize your Level Titles, go to [Formatting Syles](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/formatting-styles)

These Settings are **necessary** if you want to **export levels**. Go to [Export and Publish Levels](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/export-and-publish-levels)
 to know more

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FGdcAm6FLFYxIVSAVCS7v%252FSem%2520T%25C3%25ADtulo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0b47dbff-1a02-4402-93a0-d83db9526981&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=64183076&sv=2)

Editor - Level Settings Tab (Top)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fdg2zw5i6JFhcWgy0fYfg%252FSem%2520T%25C3%25ADtulo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3efbb0a-5c09-401c-8b08-2c4f5f7599c4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9b890f98&sv=2)

Editor - Level Settings Tab (Bottom)

# Access the Editor | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/access-the-editor.md)
.

When you turn on the game, you will see this screen:

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F1wqHiEOm6dohRhSTwRYq%252F1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5eb12cd1-6f1e-4eaf-8a7b-34f26815ec8c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bf45005f&sv=2)

"A Dance of Fire and Ice" Starting Screen

Follow the path of floor tiles into the **portal** that indicates Level Editor.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FnqpReferuVBFUZ7yPEAr%252F1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D115d6b1a-c549-4ea6-a6d7-9f95d0e65b34&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f22950e7&sv=2)

Main Screen - Mode Selection

You can also use `Ctrl + Shift + E` to quickly access the editor.

And there we go, you are on the game's editor!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FSYqaa8TNHhPVDd5wkbco%252F1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D703c663e-08cf-4cf9-bb04-de074bdd47a8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c1878b6a&sv=2)

Editor Screen

[NextLocate levels files](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/locate-levels-files)

# Locate levels files | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/locate-levels-files.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/locate-levels-files#opening-your-most-recent-level)

• Opening your most recent level


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This will open your **last viewed** level in the editor, regardless of its creator.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F8oLHRquojzIAulcNaKbY%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6297b9b7-fab7-418e-90eb-66d016f3e990&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=49046cd3&sv=2)

Editor Top Bar - Open "filename"

When you open the **Top bar menu**, you can access your most recent level. This will trigger a **warning** to ensure that your current level editing won't be lost by switching levels.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FSUfF7e7bh1lau6BsOthN%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D66a3b2cd-5fbc-4120-8e1e-45ab012b89ca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4b74009a&sv=2)

Editor - Opening a new level warning

You can now begin editing your most recent opened level!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F0K9ROxcKY1evQtWLyEfq%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7adca6e-1539-4367-ba2e-f1f2b8d61df2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8f374b4c&sv=2)

Editor - Most recent level

* * *

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/locate-levels-files#opening-a-level-saved-on-your-computer)

• Opening a level saved on your computer


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Open the **Top Bar Menu**, and then select the **Open...** Option. This time, the game will open **your computer explorer**.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FFJlY6zLXniw5vpyiWX8x%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D83d7e843-4c6e-4d74-ac53-6f2739f47684&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c40dacbf&sv=2)

Editor - Windows Explorer

Select the level you would like to open, and the editor will start loading everything for you!

_You might have to look for the folder where you typically storage your .adofai levels._

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FJzDu7rMfKM40D1r3bt4X%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D791dfdb8-0003-4d54-bb91-75c2eaa26352&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e9a2c883&sv=2)

Editor - UFO level

* * *

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/locate-levels-files#opening-a-level-with-a-url)

• Opening a level with a URL


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**File Storage Websites** - _(Use these to storage your levels on the cloud)_[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/locate-levels-files#file-storage-websites-use-these-to-storage-your-levels-on-the-cloud)

*   Discord -> https://cdn.discordapp.com/attachments/"serverid"/"channelid"/file.zip
    
*   Catbox -> [https://catbox.moe](https://catbox.moe/)
    
*   MediaFire -> [https://www.mediafire.com/](https://www.mediafire.com/)
    

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/locate-levels-files#not-recommended)

NOT RECOMMENDED

*   Google Drive -> [~https://drive.google.com/~](https://drive.google.com/)
    
*   Mega -> [~https://mega.nz/~](https://mega.nz/)
    
*   OneDrive -> [~https://onedrive.live.com~](https://onedrive.live.com/)
    
*   Degoo -> [~https://degoo.com/~](https://degoo.com/)
    

You can open .zip files from the web directly onto the editor. To do this, go to the **Top Menu bar**, select **Open with URL...**, and paste the URL from the storage website to download the file onto your computer. This will open the level immediately on the editor, ready to edit.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FF8RSTSlev64nQi06kfoV%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df6d54ce9-001b-469e-8bda-22e23ed3888f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=941e5310&sv=2)

Editor Top Bar - URL Level Download

Opened Levels might not be compatible with your current game version. Always check your version and match it with the level file version to ensure everything works.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Ff64BgpsNRlyXdL54ghnP%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1e844ea6-bb73-4f53-80c9-e4293260fbed&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fcb14798&sv=2)

Editor - URL level loaded

* * *

[PreviousAccess the Editor](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/access-the-editor)
[NextName and Save Levels](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/name-and-save-levels)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Song Settings | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/song-settings.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/song-settings#list-of-settings)

List of Settings


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setting Name

Type Validation

Description

Filename

Audio file

Audio file for your level music (_Accepts .ogg .mp3 .wav .aiff .aif extensions) (Ideal: .ogg)_

Beats per minute

Numerical

Starting speed of your level

Volume

Numerical

% of volume your music will be played at start

Offset

Numerical

Delay in milliseconds, added to your gameplay start so it matches the audio timing

Pitch

Numerical

Playback speed of the level in % _(100% = Original speed)_

Hitsound

Multiple selection

Sound each tile will play when hit

Sound Volume

Numerical

% of volume each hitsound will be played

Countdown ticks

Numerical

Number of beats in the countdown timer until the level's starting beat

To calculate your Beats per minute and Offset correctly, head over [Finding the Correct BPM & Offset](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset)
. These are **essential values** for your level creation!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FY3t8I9Fh57ceRVLPlf58%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D81e6a373-12f1-4984-92be-786e34437e53&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d78418cf&sv=2)

Editor - Song Settings Tab

[PreviousEditor Menu List](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list)
[NextLevel Settings](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/level-settings)

Last updated 1 year ago

\`\`\`

\`ask\` is the immediate question: it should be specific, self-contained, and written in natural language.
\`goal\` is optional and describes the broader end goal you are ultimately trying to accomplish on behalf of the user. GitBook uses it to tailor the answer towards what is most useful for that goal.

# How to use & search the Guide

## • \*\*Color and Index Format:\*\*

\*\*\*Here are some pointers to help you learn more efficiently\*\*\*

{% hint style="info" %}
\*\*Bold - Keywords\*\*

\*Italic - Additional information\*

<mark style="color:blue;">Blue - Links</mark>

<mark style="color:purple;">Purple - Editor Guide Pages</mark>

<mark style="color:orange;">Orange - In-game Sections</mark>

<mark style="color:yellow;">Yellow - Keyboard Shortcuts</mark>

<mark style="color:red;">Red - Negative Feedback</mark>

<mark style="color:green;">Green - Positive Feedback</mark>
{% endhint %}

\*\*\*

## • Using the search bar (Detailed search)

For detailed results with specific terms, use the search bar at the top right of this guide website.

<figure><img src="/files/HrP7truJeK3S7SKhGeIO" alt="" width="563"><figcaption><p>Editor Guide - Using the search bar</p></figcaption></figure>

{% hint style="info" %}
Access the \*\*search menu\*\* at any time by pressing the <mark style="color:yellow;">\`Ctrl\`</mark>\`+\`<mark style="color:yellow;">\`K\`</mark> shortcut.
{% endhint %}

When you add your topics, the guide will search for both \*\*page names\*\* and \*\*keywords\*\* within each topic to find all results according to your search.

<figure><img src="/files/CbiLCQaBc3Dp52xuTR9T" alt="" width="563"><figcaption><p>Editor Guide - Search Results (Red: <mark style="color:red;">Page name</mark> ~ Orange: <mark style="color:orange;">Keyword</mark>)</p></figcaption></figure>

Choose the best option to quickly navigate directly to that page!

<figure><img src="/files/Jax0lJVUS6QdtvhdNQyk" alt="" width="563"><figcaption><p>Editor Guide - Searched Page</p></figcaption></figure>

\*\*\*

## • Using the Directory / Left Tab (Step by Step search)

For searches where you're unsure of what to look for, but have a general idea of your goal, it's beneficial to explore step by step. Navigate through information to find your golden nugget of knowledge.

<figure><img src="/files/gexIPRadhiuE6cgNm85p" alt="" width="563"><figcaption><p>Editor Guide - Directory (Red: <mark style="color:red;">Left Page List</mark> ~ Green: <mark style="color:green;">Page Linking</mark> ~ Yellow: <mark style="color:yellow;">Search bar</mark>)</p></figcaption></figure>

Each main topic page includes illustrative page link cards that help visualize content related to each subtopic found within the pages.

<figure><img src="/files/K5WqtcKkNjb1wXzcTyIU" alt="" width="563"><figcaption><p>Editor Guide - Step by Step search (Red: <mark style="color:red;">Head Page</mark> ~ Green: <mark style="color:green;">Sub Page</mark>)</p></figcaption></figure>

Finally, as you research everything necessary for your upcoming Top Level creation, persistently apply this method until you reach your desired topic!

# Types of Validation | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/types-of-validation.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/types-of-validation#list-of-validations)

List of Validations


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Validation Type

Examples

Numerical

3524, -14, 0.43

Text

Lorem Ipsum, array1, d4rk3n

Multiple Selection

(DropList with multiple choices)

Radio Selection

(Few choices where one is always on)

File

main.adofai, music.ogg, img.png

Hex Code

123456ff, 00ff0000, 542199ff

It is important to follow the introduction of data with the **correct type** on each setting, otherwise, the settings values won't work!

_Some settings might require two types of data to fully work._

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setting Name

Type Validation

Description

Background Color

Hex Code

Color range value for the background color

Show Tutorial Background pattern

Radio Selection

Choose between showing the background pattern or not in your levels

Tutorial Background pattern color

Hex Code

Color range value for the background pattern

Tutorial Background shape

Multiple Selection

Remove or use different variants of the background shapes in your levels

Tutorial Background shape color

Hex Code

Color range value for the background shapes

Background Image

Image File

Image to act as the background

Image Color

Hex Code

Parallax

Numerical

Indicate both X & Y values to displace the background from the player's POV

Display Mode

Multiple Selection

Select different forms of background placement

Radio Selection

Indicate if you allow to smooth digitally the background of your level

Lock Rotation

Radio Selection

Indicate if you allow the background to rotate with the camera

Loop Background

Radio Selection

Indicate if you allow the background image to repeat itself to fill its outside area

Scaling Ratio

Numerical

How much zoom, in %, the background will have

# Finding the Correct BPM & Offset | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#understanding-why-using-the-correct-offset-and-bpm-is-important)

Understanding why using the correct Offset and BPM is important


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

While making levels, we often find our songs to be quite difficult to work with because the bases for level creation aren't set automatically for us when adding the song file. This is because every level requires some **preparation** before the actual level editing occurs

So, here is what you should do before anything else when adding your song file to the level:

*   Find the **correct BPM** - _beats per minute_
    
*   Find the **correct Offset** - _how delayed the game starts compared to the song start_
    

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#how-to-find-the-ideal-bpm-for-your-song)

How to find the ideal BPM for your song

If possible, ask the artist who made the song for its BPM, which will save a considerable amount of time.

Unfortunately, the ADOFAI editor **does not include** any tools to help you find the song's BPM, so here are some external websites you can use instead:

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#bpm-finders)

• BPM Finders

[](https://www.beatsperminuteonline.com/)

![Cover](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FizKiWCHwcD1HVjbf7EFV%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd5e515e-0b92-435d-895f-0c66fb3a6f5f&width=490&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=82593484&sv=2)

**Beatsperminuteonline**

`_Tapper_`

[How to use](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#beatsperminuteonline)

[](https://www.all8.com/tools/bpm.htm)

![Cover](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FUHuptvtXizUo4Y6KEVud%252FEndlessRealityAll8BPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db227784e-ca39-41a2-b74a-b1f1b00b3832&width=490&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6b2289c5&sv=2)

**All8 Tap for Beats Per Minute**

`_Tapper_`

[How to use](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#all8-tap-for-beats-per-minute)

[](https://vocalremover.org/key-bpm-finder)

![Cover](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FSSG9LrvTTRo5jEn0P9Yr%252FTapTempoMegaSphereHostility.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D79732d41-2946-487a-9bdc-c192527fb6dc&width=490&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=96901b2c&sv=2)

**VocalRemover**

`_Tapper_`

[How to use](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#vocalremover-tap-tempo)

[](https://arrowvortex.ddrnl.com/)

![Cover](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FS9LF5irTJctG86nLlyx9%252FArrowVortex%2520AutoFind%2520BPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9cdec1e9-1807-4775-a764-18d49b6ebf3a&width=490&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=561b041e&sv=2)

**ArrowVortex**

`_AutoFinder_`

[How to use](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#arrowvortex)

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#how-to-find-the-correct-offset-for-your-level)

How to find the correct offset for your level

Unfortunately, the ADOFAI editor **does not include** any tools to help you find the song's offset, so here are some external tools you can use instead:

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#offset-finders)

• Offset Finders

[](https://www.audacityteam.org/download/windows/)

![Cover](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fhv7NbdukRpLrE1z8sdld%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9ff0d8e-05f0-4d40-9f90-ac0f8f856063&width=490&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e97b6e38&sv=2)

**Audacity**

[How to use](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#audacity)

You can always **change** the pitch down of your level, to test how accurate your BPM and offset are. Just remember to switch it back to 100% when you are done

_Both these methods are only as accurate as their user's precision. If you still have trouble finding either the Offset or the BPM, ask someone from the community to help. It's always great to have second opinions!_

* * *

#### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#beatsperminuteonline)

• beatsperminuteonline

How to use:[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#how-to-use)

**\[1\]** After entering the website, it's important to **play your song** in the background, as this website will follow the **user's input** to the beat.

**\[2\]** Press any key _or your mouse on the BPM button_ and try to be consistent with your taps. This is where the bpm counter will present you with a number that should be your song's bpm. _Try to do at least 40 consistent presses._

**\[3\]** Use the value you acquired on the Song Settings - Beats per minute, and you are all ready!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Ft7x0ncpSpyWDdewBYAgk%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8a8de151-6949-42d2-ac5d-05d354f75025&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e9944df4&sv=2)

**\[1\]** Beatsperminuteonline Website

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FgVNyn75jFVoziE7pyPfl%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1876ca8a-8f7d-4ad3-850e-f3a625c36afc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e037c35&sv=2)

**\[2\]** Beatsperminuteonline - BPM found

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fzm5yC4iHQ1JFM9QIkYw2%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3c881a57-6ce5-4cc2-922b-252d718430bc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b6e856f0&sv=2)

**\[3\]** Game Editor, Song Settings - Correct BPM

* * *

#### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#all8-tap-for-beats-per-minute)

•All8 Tap for Beats Per Minute

II. How to use:[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#ii.-how-to-use)

**\[1\]** This one works in a very similar way to Beatsperminuteonline, however, it is more minimalistic and straight to the point. It's mostly a question of preference, so feel free to try both and see which suits you better.

**\[2\]** Press any key _or your mouse on the BPM button_ and try to be consistent with your taps. This is where the bpm counter will present you with a number that should be your song's bpm. _Try to do at least 40 consistent presses._

**\[3\]** Use the value you acquired on the Song Settings - Beats per minute, and you are all ready!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FAn4rdQRqusu6rASd3xNf%252FScreenshot%25202023-07-09%2520at%252014-10-25%2520Tap%2520for%2520Beats%2520Per%2520Minute%2520BPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6892a3ff-53bb-4283-805d-790839fc658a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ece6439b&sv=2)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FUHuptvtXizUo4Y6KEVud%252FEndlessRealityAll8BPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db227784e-ca39-41a2-b74a-b1f1b00b3832&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6b2289c5&sv=2)

**\[2\]** All8 Tap for Beats Per Minute - BPM found

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FY9zEkIHcT1UkHStwgADi%252FEndlessRealityBPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4b257c0c-1d53-48ba-9d5c-f7c4058c6ef8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cfa20bcc&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#vocalremover-tap-tempo)

• VocalRemover Tap Tempo

III. How to use:[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#iii.-how-to-use)

**\[1\]** VocalRemover has a BPM autofinder and a BPM tapper. Only the BPM tapper will be covered.

**\[2\]** In the "_Tap Tempo_" function, is it required by the user to press space at least 20 times in the rhythm of the song to have the estimated BPM, but the user can do more if they want a more consistent result. This is more precise than the last two, but in exchange, requires a higher precision of the user to get an accurate estimation.

**\[3\]** Use the value you acquired on the Song Settings - Beats per minute, and you are all ready!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fq6f9URpzYJbo5BHU3fZb%252FVocalRemover%2520Page.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2c72d59-635e-4fd3-80e8-d0aa9c48658a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3aa6ee7e&sv=2)

**\[1\]** VocalRemover Website - Song Key and BPM Finder

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FSSG9LrvTTRo5jEn0P9Yr%252FTapTempoMegaSphereHostility.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D79732d41-2946-487a-9bdc-c192527fb6dc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=96901b2c&sv=2)

**\[2\]** BPM acquired after tapping on the rhythm

* * *

#### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#arrowvortex)

• ArrowVortex

IV. How to use:[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#iv.-how-to-use)

**\[1\]** ArrowVortex is mainly a program made for making charts for 4k rhythm games, like StepMania, Osu!Mania, Quaver, Eterna, etc.; but it can actually be useful to find the BPM of songs for other games, like in this case, ADOFAI.

**\[2\]** To download ArrowVortex, just simply use one of the download options provided by its website, and extract the .rar file. When you open ArrowVortex, it should look like this. _(Picture below)_

**\[3\]** To find the BPM of the song you will use, you are firstly to open the song file in the program. To do so, click the "_File_" button (I), then the "_Open_" button (II). After that, find the song file in your selected directory and open it.

_Press_ `F3` _to hear beat ticks, that correspond with the current BPM._

**\[4\]** After opening the song in the program, click on the "_Tempo_" button, then "_Adjust sync_".

**\[5\]** This will bring you to the "_ADJUST SYNC_" settings, where the ArrowVoltex has a built-in feature to automatically find the BPM of a song, when pressing "_Find BPM_".

_If the BPM the autofinder gave was an rational number, the safest thing to do is_ _**use the nearest integer number**__._

**\[6\]** After finding the BPM, put the value you acquired on the Song Settings - Beats per minute, and you are all ready!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FiVP9qOXt8kQBCq6Ndk23%252FScreenshot%25202023-07-09%2520at%252017-16-41%2520ArrowVortex.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dce180dc3-1484-44e5-b7f4-5730559f05de&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cba91e8b&sv=2)

**\[1\]** ArrowVortex Website

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FWrunOAXFR2TaYR7cP2vz%252FArrowVortex%2520Main%2520Menu.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc54445ed-e4ba-43ef-8361-fe47e1d81876&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=86cb5ad2&sv=2)

**\[4\]** Order of buttons to press

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FS9LF5irTJctG86nLlyx9%252FArrowVortex%2520AutoFind%2520BPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9cdec1e9-1807-4775-a764-18d49b6ebf3a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=561b041e&sv=2)

**\[5\]** "_ADJUST SYNC_" Menu

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FzKX4ImqcjoYdqn6uCl8K%252FCaptura%2520de%2520tela%25202023-07-09%2520182618.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45152759-5b81-4498-970f-860d00d87bc1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f75be7ba&sv=2)

**\[6\]**

* * *

#### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#audacity)

• Audacity

V. How to use:[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset#v.-how-to-use)

**\[1\]** To find an offset that works in the game, you have to take into consideration:

*   Where do you want the gameplay to start? When the music starts, or at a later point in the song?
    

**\[2\]** To **add a song**, simply draw any audio file into the program, and a screen with the track's audio waves should appear.

**\[3\]** If you notice any gap between the start and the blue waves, that means your song has offset. To find out, click on the top of the gap and use the **Zoom + tool** to take a closer look.

**\[4\]** Finally, use your **key arrows,** or **mouse click** to place as close as possible, to the first blue high wave, to find a close-to-perfect offset from the **start** of your song.

This value will match the start of your gameplay level (_make sure to copy the time that is in milliseconds_), use that value on the Song Settings - Offset, and you are all ready!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FIUDGV6IGq6DdyFrRoViJ%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3cea3e8f-3998-478e-b529-62c84f3cede8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1717a28e&sv=2)

**\[1\]** Audacity - Main Screen

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FJ2dsI1Ut9dAOfnrievEE%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91ab20ad-56b1-4793-ba17-da1dfa1a3537&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dd6623e3&sv=2)

**\[2\]** Audacity - Track display

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FoJ0xDyqpg5wOu9ghsBBi%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9aff41a9-bd73-492f-812a-d3db1041d8cc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35fde312&sv=2)

# Camera Settings | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/camera-settings.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/camera-settings#list-of-settings)

List of Settings


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setting Name

Type Validation

Description

Relative to

Multiple Selection

Select which point your camera is focusing

Position

Numerical

Offset Position on X & Y from the camera point relative to, in tiles

Rotation

Numerical

Value, in degrees, of how much the camera turns around itself

Zoom

Numerical

How much, in %, the camera focus something

Pulse camera at tiles

Radio Selection

Indicate if you allow the camera to pulse everytime you press a hit while playing

# Workshop and Level Hunting | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/workshop-and-level-hunting.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/workshop-and-level-hunting#access-the-games-steam-workshop)

Access the game's Steam Workshop


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Steam Workshop has vast other game content available for players to subscribe to and play as they like. To access the ADOFAI's workshop, head over to your game section on your Steam library and press Workshop

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fmq7U5t7q83I5xPMDZBxM%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df3f856cc-6940-49d7-86fd-818ca4f60d2b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d769c861&sv=2)

Steam Library - Game Tab

The game's workshop is now open. From Discussions, Screenshots, Videos, Guides, and much more, every piece of content can be found here, including all levels made by other players

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FGZHYvAk9MxoOvzedGzMh%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D85307d4c-a9c3-48e5-ae81-9f0ed9b2d304&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=16ebbbe1&sv=2)

Steam - ADOFAI workshop

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/workshop-and-level-hunting#finding-new-levels)

Finding new levels


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/workshop-and-level-hunting#by-name)

• By name

To search for a specific artist, song, or level creator, write their name into the workshop search bar. All level content that matches your description, should appear right under

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FZbJv7T1FVbWU2exdctPi%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D02241437-f2a9-41a0-b470-2d952a67f5b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=defb9871&sv=2)

Workshop - Search Bar

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FpChTxbo8rnNtnjqCjfea%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D141acf53-b236-427b-ae9e-a447280eb729&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=938db892&sv=2)

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/workshop-and-level-hunting#by-most-recent-uploaded)

• By most recent uploaded

Searching for new uploaded levels is simple. Under the search bar, there is a section for popular workshop tabs such as Most Popular, Last Updated, etc. In there, click the "Most Recent" to head over to the most recent uploaded levels section

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FpeVV7fXXMLEJF9cObAdk%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D10998634-6082-4f36-a8ab-cbcff4c45a3b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c41d8107&sv=2)

Workshop - Browse Recent Items by Tag

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FeFwxxE2B9ubXgmNgkDcU%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D33f5a92b-00d8-4757-a863-e0a32cb0513f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=16fe3c13&sv=2)

Workshop - Most Recent Levels

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/workshop-and-level-hunting#by-most-popular)

• By most popular

As you open the game's workshop, you will be presented with the Top 9 most Popular levels of the week

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FvBskqApvVSzixvWrx7rZ%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9138ceb0-f912-4bf2-be72-76dbf3febb52&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8f03948c&sv=2)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FGGlqaAHIf3lSrYF3Kixn%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De86ccd36-5516-4041-a342-affb746d0a26&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=29bb95ba&sv=2)

Workshop - Over Time Period List

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/workshop-and-level-hunting#by-difficulty-and-content-available)

• By Difficulty and Content available

Levels can be searched by a difficult setting (steam evaluation, not gems) and/or their content available inside each level. Pressing any of the available options will direct you to the levels that meet the same criteria

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FTpnILfadEJzNLwmGARZm%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7796d05e-a4ce-4b1d-813d-3232685fe121&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f88e9b38&sv=2)

Workshop - Browse by Difficulty / Content

Each setting will use the most popular of the week as the second criteria on finding levels with a selected Difficulty and/or Content

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fa2GSQKNTHDQLqIrD4O4o%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6383978c-63ff-459c-a118-f58415bf1422&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8741c799&sv=2)

Workshop - Browse by Content

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/workshop-and-level-hunting#access-your-level-files-on-the-workshop)

Access your level files on the Workshop


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Your released levels can be found on the workshop inside the files you have posted. Just click "Your files" and then "Files you've posted"

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FYHjxIEyFnopdiFgXgwE7%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1ac76034-68d9-44f2-a1d3-51ac0a571453&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c8e21921&sv=2)

This will not change the in-game Artist/Song content or its level description. Merely changes the steam level display

# Name and Save Levels | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/name-and-save-levels.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/name-and-save-levels#naming-rules)

• Naming Rules


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/name-and-save-levels#general-rules-for-level-naming)

‣ General rules for level naming

Naming your level is quite easy, although there are some **precautions** to take to ensure full compatibility across every OS version of the game.

*   Levels **can** contain letters (a-z), numbers (0-9), dashes (-), underscore (\_), and periods (.);
    
*   Levels permit these characters, but it is strongly advised to avoid using ampersands (&), equal signs (=), apostrophes ('), plus signs (+), commas (,), angle brackets (<,>), spaces ( ), consecutive periods (..), or any non-alphabetical symbols.
    

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FCRjyRShzgm3hSPqh3j4V%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14f00220-5f38-4ac2-85f8-fd69208edb2b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=71bf7a36&sv=2)

Explorer - Good example of naming

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fz27thj0tTSAnUNcuocBb%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd48e97c-addc-4c21-821e-4fc4dc20e1ae&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ef6d3f0&sv=2)

Explorer - Bad example of naming

* * *

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/name-and-save-levels#naming-levels-to-include-tutorials)

‣ Naming levels to include tutorials

When publishing levels, the workshop allows you to add tutorials to your levels. This is possible by including one file for each tutorial, grouping them with the _LevelNameTutorialNumber.adofai_ format

**Levelname** must match your main file's name, so the game can associate the level with its tutorials, e.g., fragor1.adofai

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FN9ocHkPBNjrSfcBRcfvb%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb327356-a2d8-4e29-a30d-1426975fea8a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ec48474c&sv=2)

Game Editor - Tutorial levels info

* * *

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/name-and-save-levels#saving-levels)

• Saving Levels


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/name-and-save-levels#saving-current-level)

‣ Saving current Level

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fu2ZyTPkX0VWn7jMySvzm%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D539fb726-1cce-4be3-b6af-13db49493758&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=66b053a8&sv=2)

Editor Screen

When opening the editor, it is best to first **save your level** to create the necessary files from the very start. When saving, two files will be **stored** in your desired storage location:

*   main.adofai
    
*   backup.adofai
    

The .adofai file format is used to save all of your levels.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FUIh6HF7B5bM1tsO5KMSc%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28d68be5-076b-4390-8293-a6c06369cb77&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a8dc27ba&sv=2)

Editor - Top Menu Bar

To save your files, use your **mouse** to click on the **Top Menu Bar** where the 💾 icon is. A drop-down list should appear with several options. For this part, we are focusing only on the **Save** and **Save As...** options.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FORS74Xxid6Z7WbkgEMqZ%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D93d4ae53-bad7-4d65-a346-241c22520987&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=32a49e7a&sv=2)

Editor - Top Menu Bar opened

Regarding the **Save** option, it saves your current level progress. You can do this at any time after making changes to the level you are currently editing.

You can also use `Ctrl + S` to save your current level.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FvRYgVkLHyliUBHXxcKbf%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D090b3b0e-5ff1-41f7-99ca-7f9717959064&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3cb0edbc&sv=2)

Editor - Top Menu Bar showing the level with a saved name

When **saving** for the **first time**, your OS will request to save your file on your default directory. Make sure to select your desired location before confirming the first save.

* * *

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/name-and-save-levels#saving-a-new-copy-of-the-current-level)

‣ Saving a new copy of the current Level

The **Save As...** option creates a new file, unlike the **Save** option, which only updates the file you are currently working on.

When you select this option, a new window appears. You can use the explorer tools on your computer to choose where to save your level and to properly name your file.

All your decor, videos and files will be automatically storage on the new level location.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F1Pa7oJ4BnYRiPLU7A3kV%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44f8082d-c5ef-4ea2-b632-927a5ceaae1e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b73c669&sv=2)

Windows Explorer - Saving

You can also use `Ctrl + Shift + S` to save your level into a new file.

Remember to include all the files, such as decorations and song audio files, when exporting levels onto .zip files.

* * *

[NextFinding the Correct BPM & Offset](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset)
