# Tile Placement | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement.md)
.

When it comes to constructing your level, the editor allows you to input each tile using the keyboard. There are also several methods to custom input an angle into the game. Before we continue, here is how the image will be subtitled for your understanding:

*   **White Letters** - Keyboard Shortcut for tile placement
    
*   **Yellow Lines and Angles** - 90º Separation placement and their associated angles
    
*   **Blue Lines and Angles** \- 45º Separation placement and their associated angles
    
*   **Green Lines and Angles** - 30º Separation placement and their associated angles
    
*   Red Lines and Angles - 15º Separation placement and their associated angles
    

Let's now learn how to start counting angles **according to the planet's rotation**. All examples will be based out of a `4/4` Tempo Signature, which is the most commonly used around most songs. Each angle will be counting from 0º at its most right side radius, turning counter-clockwise and increasing this number until one full lap around is complete, where it goes back to 0º

Learning this angle measure is efficient as your level will register angles into your Angle Data portion on your level files. Learn more about this on [Surgery](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/surgery)
 Page

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement#id-90o-angles)

90º Angles


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Starting from the basics, 90º placements are the simplest to use, as they represent our on-beats and off-beats of the song

So let's consider that every time we hit 0º, we are doing 1 beat into the song beat

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FI8rQlPQXHu30Ea7Py8Xg%252FCompass%25200%2520degrees.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1f9557f7-ed8f-46cb-9629-c3943ec23ffe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d224b23a&sv=2)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet where each sheet beat, equals the start of an angle (0º degrees)

#### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement#example-1)

• Example 1

According to the game tile values, each tile represents an angle. Said angle is always base out of a counter-clockwise rotation from each beat, meaning 1 beat equals a starting point of an angle value.

With this in mind, every time you place a tile that isn't at beat start, its angle value will increase depending on how its angle ends, based from the beat start position.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FpxzkM1K2zzRApGccGap6%252F90%2520angles.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D99dd1a03-904d-4449-bde3-7e4e9ee7a553&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=727c9511&sv=2)

Angle Rotation - 90º Splits

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fq1T5X1mcShMi5ejiU10P%252FCompass%25200%2520degrees%2520with%2520offbeats.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D77a6404d-c384-4d4a-8719-e97f70f6e71d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4360a428&sv=2)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, now with off-beat indicators

These vertical angles (90º and 270º) are what we call off-beats, meaning they can occur in between each beat

#### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement#example-2)

• Example 2

Notice how the last horizontal tile had an angle of 180º? This is due to the origin point of the track being left to right, meaning this angle has a value of half a circle = 180º

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FcSMroFP8KqrX4mTA5a8q%252FCompass%252090%2520degrees.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca83b1ef-8f4d-4a19-95d2-a6df6dfeff25&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c18550f3&sv=2)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, using off-beats

#### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement#example-3)

• Example 3

Same logic applies here, each angle doing down has to turn a radius angle from the right to left, so 1 and a half circle = 270º

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FcTYMTaY1p7SDyQpRDmhp%252FCompass%2520270%2520degrees.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D75581d69-bb89-42b7-8817-2e415bdfbe85&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7ff8ef9e&sv=2)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, using long off-beats

#### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement#example-4)

• Example 4

This case is a bit tricky. Each angle, compared to the last one, is a 90º different, however, when counting angles always remember to do it counter-clockwise, always starting from the beat line radius angle.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FmJ7an9aln6sS6qIPjKHP%252FCompass%2520squares%2520degrees.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7d0d9bc6-5e79-4ed9-9998-1851406c74d9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=af7d73de&sv=2)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, mixing on-beats and off-beats

In conclusion, the angles presented in the square are 0º, 90º, 180º, 270º and 0º again. These are the angles the game file will record to make the square form.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement#id-45o-angles)

45º Angles


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now that we got the hang of on-beats and off-beats, let's add one more beat in between those. We now can play 4 beats inside each sheet beat. Each beat now is considered a sixteenth note

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FBitE6ywsoU2EEpphnhdk%252FCompass%252045%2520degrees%2520with%2520offbeats.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D78b45098-7ce0-481c-a34f-1c077bb70d6d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2b85556&sv=2)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet with 4 splits of 45º each sheet beat

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FxwheWY5SHGJQ8leAoXx6%252F45%2520angles.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c507961-754d-4f33-8829-97af5308cdf6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8aaa78c1&sv=2)

Angle Rotation - 45º Splits

#### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement#example-1-1)

• Example 1

For this example, you can see that we created a tile that doesn't go fully horizontal, nor vertical. Sixteenths splitting allow notes to be played in between on-beats and off-beats

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FwpQp4CqfewRXAhguxzcB%252FCompass%252045%2520degrees.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D78cd602c-40ef-4764-82e2-d4d1fe143fbc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6e0d2dda&sv=2)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, showing 45º angles

#### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement#example-2-1)

• Example 2

This is how a curve using the previous sixteenths angles would look like. As the sum of some sixteenths angles is equal to some off-beat and on-beat notes, those tiles also appear in the sixteenth curve to support the rhythm

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FZir2QlirphupsPfZ7lLb%252FCompass%252045%2520curve%2520degrees.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb05791f-8505-473d-992e-677cf3d35484&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6a1dff24&sv=2)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, curve tile using 45º angles

#### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement#example-3-1)

• Example 3

Following the logic of a square pattern, we can build one using only intervals from the sixteenth placement, making all angles be hit in between on-beats and off-beats

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FFrzbENWWSJfU2NhDgu4P%252FCompass%252045-135%2520squares%2520degrees.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1314dcf-e4f3-4cac-b1c1-b5e3f68bf9a7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=73cb7ee0&sv=2)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, making squares of sixteenth

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement#id-30o-angles)

30º Angles


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These angles are mostly used for swing style of music, but the tile placement logic is the same. Take in consideration the 45º angles, where we placed 1 beat in between each on-beat and off-beat. This time, we are placing two beats in between each, rather than one, allowing us to count 24 beats in each sheet compared to the 16 beats from the 45º angles.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FmMTiV3WLMHZZyfPGfedo%252FCompass%252030%2520degrees%2520with%2520offbeats.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D344fb9d5-56d4-4728-a8e6-0aaf7252c276&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1f1310c0&sv=2)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet with 6 splits of 30º each sheet beat

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FU0y0mX0VoPlxHJI97Y25%252F30%2520angles.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9b647b4e-f255-49bd-a84d-32f3c607aade&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fb60cfba&sv=2)

Angle Rotation - 30º Splits

You can access these shortcut tiles by holding `Shift` during the placement

#### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement#example-1-2)

• Example 1

Similar to 45º angle example, you can see that we created a tile that doesn't go fully horizontal, nor vertical, however since we have two beats between those angles, we can go beyond a perfect middle angle, but one that equally divided more to the horizontal angle, and another more to the vertical angle.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FkPtbfNvgoCUX7hKn6A0l%252FCompass%252030%2520degrees.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D98cca718-eb7e-4869-abc0-a1f08fbad3f3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d97e18e2&sv=2)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, showing 30º angles

#### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement#example-2-2)

• Example 2

A curve that fits the 4/4 tempo is only possible if we use angles above 90º, which means 30º angles will be taking too long, requiring more than one sheet of 4/4 tempo. So we are using what we call the Hexagons (Curves made out of 120º angles). For this example, you can see how a swing beat can interact with a full rotation angle tile.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FH12Jzgmj5rJWyngtSae2%252FCompass%252060%2520curve%2520degrees.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dede74ac7-934e-4da8-9f80-389e6f792993&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6dd517f3&sv=2)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, curve half hexagon using 60º angles

#### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement#example-3-2)

• Example 3

Making squares on swing tempos can be a bit tricky. These come from a mix of on-beats and swings beats, to create the jazzy gameplay style.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F38CoeYMzFgsIiZNGM4sx%252FCompass%252060-240%2520squares%2520degrees.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D41d4f63e-f841-4b50-aaaf-5de1bdb6f5fa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=838cd690&sv=2)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, making squares of 60º angles

Take into consideration that we are using the same angles for both the on-beats used, but alternatives to these angles are possible too. So get creative and place some tiles around, get creating!

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement#id-15o-angles)

15º Angles


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

As an extra demonstration, the game allows you to fast input 15º Angles

You can access these shortcut tiles by holding `Shift``+` `` ` `` during the placement

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FL6DwGdkdFqZcxegBxrom%252F15%2520angles.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3a350103-9cc2-453a-8662-1c86db6f3807&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3cf5947f&sv=2)

Angle Rotation - 15º Splits

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement#custom-angles)

Custom Angles


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If any of these methods won't do for your levels, you can customize the exact angle you're looking for. To insert a custom angle, press the angle button after selecting the tile you want to insert the angle from.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Ft9LsrB6D8qre5Vuw4Ha1%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D190aee42-1821-406e-a2a6-bdbadf05a5d6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1b807202&sv=2)

Editor - Insert Angle Button

From there, your options should look like the image below. Simply write your angle inside the text box, and click in one of the two tile types, to add the desired angle. (Regular tile or Mid-spin tile)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FZLf5j9Dw75trsErUBugy%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dac583c5d-38b3-4c17-a5b1-8f9decb092d8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=61d98e3e&sv=2)

Editor - Select type of tile and angle text box

As you can see from the image below, one 15º angle tile was added to your track. This angle was the calculation from the last tile position angle + your angle value, creating a 165º angle that is a **difference of 15º angle**, between your last tile and the new one!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FBj6OisGCcoSnIOME9chr%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6f69f56b-9f7e-49d9-87d4-523b0021fab0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d2d4c041&sv=2)

Editor - Inserted a tile with 15º Angle apart, based on the last tile angle. (165º on the editor file)

These angle inputs always measure clockwise from the **last tile angle position**, rather than angle 0º as explained for your Angle Data storage values. These inputs are merely informative to help place custom angles and their values are not stored based on them.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement#tile-placement-shortcuts)

# Mods Listing and Installation | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/mods-listing-and-installation.md)
.

Using mods may cause unexpected bugs and errors in the game

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/mods-listing-and-installation#how-to-prepare-your-mods-for-installation)

How to prepare your mods for installation


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mods can enhance your experience while playing the game. So we are going to teach how to install and use some of the most popular by players

1.  Head over to **newman55's GitHub** repository and download the **Unity Mod Manager** \[[Click here](https://github.com/newman55/unity-mod-manager)\
    \]
    

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FFQjYpE8uWKvC6YtmCrP0%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3350e17d-4551-40bd-9445-e8817b0a6806&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=47b4e398&sv=2)

Newman55 Github - Readme Pagination

1.  Unzip the `UnityModmanager.zip` file into your desired location
    

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FXu7oz1PPp6V3XIYj9dAg%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df3a17aad-a711-4456-97d9-deb234bd8da8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6467d668&sv=2)

File Explorer - Extracting the Unity Mod Manager

1.  Find the `UnityModManager.exe` file and run it
    
    3.1. In case you find trouble running the file due to version incompatibility, follow these steps \[[here](https://github.com/CrackThrough/ADOFAI-Mod-Installation-Guide/blob/main/eng/use-1.md#How-to-check-your-games-version)\
    \]
    

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FEivLT7IQIiPL0QWivE5g%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De0a57fe4-6b8d-4076-b95b-21d82ecd634f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ca3765b6&sv=2)

File Explorer - Running Unity Mod Manager

1.  Select the Game and the Game's Folder you want to install this Manager
    

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FmyP4iBLOWtfkn5zN2dXm%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D333393d1-6bd0-4efb-92d1-54df4affbd65&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6936404&sv=2)

Unity Mod Manager - Selecting the Game folders

4.1. For the Game, select A Dance of Fire and Ice. For the game's folder, select the main folder where your game is located, typically with the folder name "A Dance of Fire and Ice"

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FC9bGhMOMIndvQGxWTZlX%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba0bd152-33b3-492f-a1f1-738372d9c1c8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5812186b&sv=2)

File Explorer - Finding the Game Folder 1

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FpyV206naexyGe1vFcBLr%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D09c9287a-b539-4085-98c0-b201151b75e6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=243feca7&sv=2)

File Explorer - Finding the Game Folder 2

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FCfvsjZCl2hZKz6QCo90a%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D18208c0e-f87d-40ff-ac4f-013eb63e192b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1a4ac6fb&sv=2)

File Explorer - Finding the Game Folder 3

Default Steam Folder is at C:\\Program Files (x86)\\steam\\steamapps\\common\\A Dance of Fire and Ice

1.  Select the Mods Tab and drag all the .zip mod files you want into the white area and press Install Mod
    

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FvDYPzg54xDhxlSCE7kZW%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D589e160a-8387-4aa7-ad11-fcee0511507b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b84e7031&sv=2)

Unity Mod Manager - Dragging all .zip Mod Files

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FOiC6SLrYsOKq8aOvq3BT%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dccc4393c-fa76-4360-9b88-2990418f8ee0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1c949f0&sv=2)

Unity Mod Manager - Mod Status

1.  Select the Install Tab and click on Install
    

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F7wCovhZANvYV1rC01N69%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1c0e0efa-043b-45a0-b944-5a79b450bdf7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8315da42&sv=2)

Unity Mod Manager - Installing all Mods

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FKwAKjy6Y4yxzwJ2Ju9WG%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47f799b5-623f-40a8-bd9a-42838cc07b4b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=78e44bc0&sv=2)

Unity Mod Manager - Successful Installation

If everything worked correctly, all your mods should have an ok Status message on the Mod Tab and be found inside the game folder

When loading the game, the Unity Mod Manager should open automatically. Open/Close the manager window using `Ctrl + F10` at any time

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FlvSQiDb9HYRU6dpWxZJ4%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daec245ea-f50d-40a8-9c42-4bd680fb6d12&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=52a558b5&sv=2)

Game Menu - Mod Manager working and ready to use

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/mods-listing-and-installation#mod-list)

Mod List


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/mods-listing-and-installation#adofaitweaks)

[AdofaiTweaks](https://github.com/PizzaLovers007/AdofaiTweaks)

*   Provides various Quality Of Life settings, such as disabling VFX from levels, hiding judgment texts such as the "perfect!" judgment for less visual pollution, along with many other settings, and a key viewer.
    

* * *

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/mods-listing-and-installation#adofaicsl)

[AdofaiCSL](https://github.com/thijnmens/AdofaiCSL/releases/tag/V2.1.0)

*   A custom level loader for levels that weren't downloaded from the workshop. Find a guide on how to use it [here](https://github.com/thijnmens/AdofaiCSL/tree/V2.1.0)
    .
    

* * *

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/mods-listing-and-installation#release-overlay)

[Release Overlay](https://github.com/c3nb/Overlayer/releases/tag/v2.4.0)

* * *

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/mods-listing-and-installation#showbpm)

[ShowBPM](https://github.com/FLOWERs-Modding/ADOFAI_ShowBPM/releases/tag/1.2.0)

*   Shows the current BPM of the level being played, along with the _real_ BPM, displayed according to angle turns; and displays BPM changes as multipliers.
    

* * *

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/mods-listing-and-installation#progress-displayer)

[Progress Displayer](https://github.com/FLOWERs-Modding/ADOFAI_ProgressDisplayer2/releases/tag/v2.0.8)

*   Shows the progress percentage of a level throughout the gameplay.

# Surgery | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/surgery.md)
.

Surgery can break your level in ways that are not recoverable!

Please, if you are doing this, make sure to create a copy of your level before continuing

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/surgery#what-is-file-surgery)

What is File Surgery?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Surgery** is the act of changing your level from writing directly into the file, rather than using the editor interface.

As you know, whenever you save a level inside the Game Editor, a file that contains all the settings, actions, and decorations is updated. But in this case, we can do those changes over the file itself.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/surgery#what-do-i-need-to-start-the-surgery)

What do I need to start the Surgery?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

\-> A **Text Editor** software to read and edit the text file

Here are a few you can use for free:

\---> Windows Notepad _(You most likely already have this)_ ---> [Notepad++](https://notepad-plus-plus.org/downloads/)
 _(Better Notepad)_ ---> Any IDE software _(Integrated development environment)_

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/surgery#how-to-start-surgery-on-files.adofai)

How to start Surgery on files.adofai?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

First, find the location of your file. You can easily open your most recent file with the [Open the directory location window of most recent level](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/open-the-directory-location-window-of-most-recent-level)
 **Shortcut**

After that, `Mouse right-click` on top of your level and click on **Open with** and select your Text Editor of choice. For this example, we will be using Notepad++

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FTjkIi1GSAdrzSfKwgOiY%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D97f3b16d-6297-4fa4-8897-53a449d083e1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9892863&sv=2)

Notepad++ - Adofai Level Surgery Content

From here, it's a matter of adding and replacing values within each setting. Do have in mind, although you can put anything inside each setting, the game might not allow you to use them when you save and open the level file again

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/surgery#surgery-details)

Surgery Details


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Angle Data** - Every tile angle will be storage here
    

Check how to associate every tile angle on the [Tile Placement](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement)
 section

*   **Settings** - All the information about the level, descriptions and starting values of events
    

Check how to associate every level setting on the [Editor Menu List](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list)
 section

*   **Actions** - Every event added to the tiles will be set up here, including all its value settings
    

Check how to associate every action with events in the [Events](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events)
 section

*   **Decorations** - Every decoration and text added will be saved here, including all its value settings
    

Check how to associate every decoration on the [Decoration and Text Creative Format](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format)
 section

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/surgery#surgery-advantages)

Surgery advantages


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/surgery#easy-copy-paste)

Easy Copy-Paste

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/surgery#events-at-tile-0)

Events at Tile 0

[PreviousMods Listing and Installation](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/mods-listing-and-installation)
[NextKnowledge Library](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/knowledge-library)

# Track Settings | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/track-settings.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/track-settings#list-of-settings)

List of Settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setting Name

Type Validation

Description

Track Color type

Multiple Selection

Track color distribution, from tile to tile up to color fusion like rainbows

Track Color

Hex code

Color range value for the track tile color

Track Style

Multiple Selection

Track color foundation, the material of tiles, such as neon and gems

Track Texture

Image File

Image sheet texture to replace the tiles foundation's material

Track Texture zoom

Numerical

Indicate how in-detail each texture material shows on the tile foundation

Glow intesity

Numerical

Amount, in %, of glow each tile will show when hit

Track appear animation

Multiple Selection

Animation that makes tiles appear in front of the track

Beats before for animation

Numerical

How fast, in beats, for the animation to start ahead

Track disappear animation

Multiple Selection

Animation that makes tiles disappear behind the track

Beats after for animation

Numerical

How fast, in beats, for the animation to end behind

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fw6DtOwJgZoCwEKo0Uia2%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De0ec96fc-3338-4e5f-be11-b2b8fc1bd376&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c90500b3&sv=2)

Editor - Track Settings Tab

[PreviousLevel Settings](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/level-settings)

# Misc Settings | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/misc-settings.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/misc-settings#list-of-settings)

List of Settings


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setting Name

Type Validation

Description

Video Background

Video File

Video to be rolling as background while playing

Loop Video

Radio Selection

Indicate if you allow the video to loop after it ended

Offset

Numerical

How long, in miliseconds, the video takes to start playing when on the level

Tile Icon outlines

Radio Selection

Indicate if you allow the icons to have outlines

Sticky Tiles

Radio Selection

Indicate if you allow the tiles to be sticky and the tile movement forces the planets to move with them

Planet Orbit ease

Multiple Selection

Select how the planets rotate along each others

Orbit Ease parts

Multiple Selection

Select how many times you allow the planets orbit ease action on each tile hit

Ease Part behavior

Radio Selection

Indicate if you prefer the orbit ease to repeat or mirror the current tile hit

Default Text color

Hex Code

Color range value for the text you add

Default Text shadow color

Hex Code

Color range value for the shadow of the text you add

"Congratulations" text

Text

Custom text for when the player finishes the level

"Pure Perfect!" text

Text

Custom text for when the player perfects the level

For better knowledge on how to **score the difficulty** of your level, go to [Difficulty Scoring Methods](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/difficulty-scoring-methods)

# Export and Publish Levels | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/export-and-publish-levels.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/export-and-publish-levels#getting-everything-ready-for-exporting-your-levels)

Getting everything ready for exporting your levels


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After your level is complete, there is some **information** that needs to be filled, so your level is able to export to the **Steam Workshop**. Regardless, here is everything you need before being able to upload your level:

*   main.adofai (_and all its tutorial levels, if there are any_)
    
*   Song file (_and the tutorial level's songs, if there are any)_
    
*   All images and videos used as decor or background
    
*   Artist Permission License Proof (_image, document, etc. If needed)_
    

Make sure all of these files are inside the same folder on your computer before continuing

If you are using a song from any artist that was not authorized, your level might be deleted from the **Steam Workshop**, and you will be banned from uploading more files to the game's workshop.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/export-and-publish-levels#level-settings-export-form)

Level Settings Export Form


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the editor, the Left bar has a tab with the name Level Settings. All the information required to upload your levels is filled there

To understand how each line should be properly filled, check the Editor Menu List - [Level Settings](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/level-settings)
 section

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/export-and-publish-levels#artist-permission-information)

Artist permission information

Many artists have authorized ADOFAI fans to use their music in their levels. For those artists, **no new permission** is required for your level. To check which artists are available, check this link:

[![Logo](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F7thbe.at%2Ffavicon.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=22fd1eb7&sv=2)Verified Artists | 7th Beat Games7thbe.at](https://7thbe.at/verified-artists/adofai)

7th Beat Adofai Verified Artists List

Note that artists can be authorized and just permit a specific group of their songs only, so make sure to check if your level's song is available to use before continuing

In case you are trying to use an artist that was yet not verified, follow the guidelines of these links:

[![Logo](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.notion.so%2Ffront-static%2Flogo-ios.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3a4ca38a&sv=2)Verified Artist Guidelines | Notion7thbeat on Notion](https://7thbeat.notion.site/Artist-Permission-Guide-7979ab03ebca4ecaa58ed9d1e8e8207d)

7th Beat Artist Permission Request guide

[![Logo](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.notion.so%2Ffront-static%2Flogo-ios.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3a4ca38a&sv=2)Permission Template | Notion7thbeat on Notion](https://7thbeat.notion.site/Permission-Template-f9b45fdd77a24a349eadb8773fb7135f)

7th Beat Artist Permission Template Document

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/export-and-publish-levels#publishing-levels)

Publishing Levels


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To export your levels, so they can be played without having to upload them to the **Steam Workshop**, compact all the files into a .zip file and share the file with friends, communities and others through a direct link or using any recommended file storage website (Check[Locate levels files](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/locate-levels-files#opening-a-level-with-an-url)
)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FYkHFKiP9z0LEKeEaYqz6%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab482c4c-e787-4f55-bcff-5d1333946737&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9519ff45&sv=2)

Editor - Export Screen

After filling all the information correctly, click on Export, this screen should appear.

Verify each section to confirm if your level's information is valid and agree with the Steam Subscriber Agreement.

Time to publish your level. Press Publish world to **Steam Workshop**, and all the contents plus the tutorial levels you included are now on Steam Workshop!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FuCjawhoMAP13mTJIy8mX%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dceef77d6-a9b3-452f-8005-3ae2ed619083&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=183711ab&sv=2)

Editor - Level Published

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/export-and-publish-levels#updating-existing-levels-on-steam-workshop)

Updating existing levels on Steam Workshop

Same as exporting a new level, head over to the Export screen and press Update Existing to open a new screen with all your current released worlds. From there, select which level you would like to update and press Update selected world. The existing level should now be updated to everything that you changed to the existent level on your steam!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FdfkfGJtr1mnGPacDil69%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D63a25ac0-c795-4562-b1a1-1e12f79d8572&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ad0217cc&sv=2)

Editor - Updating World Levels

You can check how to **manage** your released levels and how to **look for** people's levels on [Workshop and Level Hunting](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/workshop-and-level-hunting)

[PreviousTypes of Validation](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/types-of-validation)
[NextEditor Menu List](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list)

Last updated 2 years ago

# Decorations | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/decorations.md)
.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fga1jmEQ70KhQzkPaL6Ru%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd4a31301-6884-41bd-b2bc-194ac0a5baaf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56f104d8&sv=2)

Decorations - Add Decor / Text

On the bottom of the Decorations tab, you can see two buttons. The one with a tree is to **add decorations**, the other with an `**Aa**` is to **add Text**

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/decorations#how-to-add-decorations)

How to add Decorations


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click on the **Add Decoration** button, a new tab on the right should appear, as well as a new decor on the Decorations List

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F721KlGYzKbmJrQXnqBuh%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3ce0e7cc-5a8e-4a13-840b-d993c60217be&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=62717357&sv=2)

Decorations - Default decor status

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FR2NlITNjAZNUKTZRjHEC%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D241e9bdd-8070-44ec-8323-0d2a2891f6ef&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ee4f27&sv=2)

Decorations Right Tab - Image Settings

From here, you can upload your image. Your **decor** should appear on the level now!

For more information on how to use Decorations, check the Advanced Techniques - [Decoration and Text Creative Format](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format)
 page

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/decorations#how-to-add-text)

How to add Text


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click on the **Add Text** button, and a new tab on the right should appear, as well as a new text on the Decorations List

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fn06Yqt7Qbac4DjJ3Ibbt%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad61c806-e1f8-4f22-b455-f951467d31cd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=937c83f&sv=2)

Decorations - Default text status

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FLtnuabOMcw30jAepy1oa%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df2e955cf-16af-4295-b2d4-071a47ce3675&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7559fbe0&sv=2)

Decorations Right Tab - Text Settings

The word **Text** should appear on your level now, go over the text area and change it to whatever text you want and done!

For more information on how to use Decorations Texts, check the Advanced Techniques - [Decoration and Text Creative Format](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format)
 page

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FfBNnrgaDeFWQhZChF8aT%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deca3916c-587c-43a4-8f4c-369f10db323e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=84b73f0b&sv=2)

Editor Left bar - Decorations

[PreviousMisc Settings](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/misc-settings)
[NextShortcuts Listing](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing)

# Basic Editing | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/basic-editing.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/basic-editing#list-of-shortcuts)

List of Shortcuts


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Keyboard Input

Description

`Tab`

[Create a midspin tile on the selected tile](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/basic-editing/create-a-midspin-tile-on-the-selected-tile)

`Shift + Space`

[Create a turnaround tile on the selected tile](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/basic-editing/create-a-turnaround-tile-on-the-selected-tile)

`P` or `Space`

[Play the level (level testing)](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/basic-editing/play-the-level-level-testing)

`Ctrl + P` or `Ctrl + Space`

[Play the level on the selected speed](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/basic-editing/play-the-level-on-the-selected-speed)

`Ctrl + C`

[Copy all selected tiles](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/basic-editing/copy-all-selected-tiles)

`Ctrl + X`

[Cut all selected tiles](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/basic-editing/cut-all-selected-tiles)

`Ctrl + V`

[Paste all selected tiles](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/basic-editing/paste-all-selected-tiles)

`Ctrl + Alt + V`

[Paste all selected tiles, without its decorations](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/basic-editing/paste-all-selected-tiles-without-its-decorations)

`Ctrl + Z`

[Undo last edit](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/basic-editing/undo-last-edit)

`Ctrl + Shift + Z` or `Ctrl + Y`

[Redo previous edit](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/basic-editing/redo-previous-edit)

`Mouse Scroll`

[Zoom in / out](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/basic-editing/zoom-in-out)

`Ctrl + Mouse Scroll`

[Change the play speed (by 10%)](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/basic-editing/change-the-play-speed-by-10)

`Ctrl + Shift + Mouse Scroll`

[Change the play speed precisely (by 1%)](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/basic-editing/change-the-play-speed-precisely-by-1)

_Click on each_ _Shortcut Description_ _for more information and video examples_

[PreviousShortcuts Listing](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing)
[NextCreate a midspin tile on the selected tile](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/basic-editing/create-a-midspin-tile-on-the-selected-tile)

Keyboard Input

Description

# Gameplay | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/gameplay.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/gameplay#list-of-shortcuts)

List of Shortcuts


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Keyboard Input

Description

`Esc`

[Exit Play mode](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/gameplay/exit-play-mode)

`Shift + Esc`

Description

# Editor Workflow | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow#list-of-shortcuts)

List of Shortcuts


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Keyboard Input

Description

`Ctrl + S`

[Save level](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/save-level)

`Ctrl + Shift + S`

[Save level as a new file](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/save-level-as-a-new-file)

`Ctrl + O`

[Open level](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/open-level)

`Ctrl + U`

[Open level from URL](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/open-level-from-url)

`Ctrl + Shift + O`

[Open most recent level](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/open-most-recent-level)

`Ctrl + Left Mouse Click` _"click on (Open recent) button on topbar"_

[Open the directory location window of most recent level](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/open-the-directory-location-window-of-most-recent-level)

`Ctrl + N`

[New level](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/new-level)

`Ctrl + Shift + P`

[Open Preferences](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/open-preferences)

`-` _Minus_

[Zoom camera out](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/zoom-camera-out)

`=` or `+` _Equal_ or _Plus_

[Zoom camera in](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/zoom-camera-in)

`Ctrl` `**+**` `-` _Minus_

[Zoom UI out](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/zoom-ui-out)

`Ctrl` `**+**` `=` _Equal_

[Zoom UI in](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/zoom-ui-in)

`Up Arrow`

[Cycle tile event tab (Next event)](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/cycle-tile-event-tab-next-event)

`Down Arrow`

[Cycle tile event tab (Previous event)](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/cycle-tile-event-tab-previous-event)

`Shift + Up Arrow`

[Cycle events of the same type (Next event)](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/cycle-events-of-the-same-type-next-event)

`Shift + Down Arrow`

[Cycle events of the same type (Previous event)](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/cycle-events-of-the-same-type-previous-event)

`[` _Left Square bracket_\
\
[Cycle events panel page (Next section)](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/cycle-events-panel-page-next-section)\
\
`]` _Right Square bracket_

[Cycle events panel page (Previous section)](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/cycle-events-panel-page-previous-section)

`Shift + [` _Left Square bracket_\
\
[Show first event page](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/show-first-event-page)\
\
`Shift + ]` _Right Square bracket_

[Show last event page](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/show-last-event-page)

_Click on each_ _Shortcut Description_ _for more information and video examples_

[PreviousFind tile with comment](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/bookmarks/find-tile-with-comment)
[NextSave level](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/save-level)

# Setting Values Calculation | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/setting-values-calculation.md)
.

Sometimes, a calculator may be needed to calculate some values for events, but instead of using an actual calculator for it, mathematical operations can be put directly put as values and the editor will automatically convert these operations into their results. The editor can accept **additions** ( + ), **subtractions** ( - ), **multiplications** ( \* ), **divisions** ( / ), and **parentheses** ( ).

Here's an example of how it works:

For any operations that require you to **insert a value**, you can use this method to use the editor to do the math for you! This works on any setting that accepts numerical values

[PreviousConditional Events Prep](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/conditional-events-prep)
[NextFormatting Styles](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/formatting-styles)

Last updated 11 months ago

\> For the complete documentation index, see \[llms.txt\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt). Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/level-settings.md). # Level Settings ## List of Settings | Setting Name | Type Validation | Description | | :--------------------------: | :----------------: | :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------: | | Artist | Text | Name of the composer | | Special Artist Type | Multiple Selection | Description of the license from the Music of said Artist | | Proof of artist's permission | File | Image or document proving the Artist allows the usage of their music | | Song | Text | Name of the music | | Author | Text | Name of the Level creator | | Portal Image | Image File | Image for the portal display at the custom levels list | | Level Icon | Image File | Image for the tile icon at the custom levels list | | Level Icon Color | Hex Code | Color range value for the icon image | | Song Preview Start | Numerical | The start point, in seconds, of the music during Custom Level selection | | Song Preview Duration | Numerical | How long, in seconds, the music plays when on the Custom Level selection | | Seizure Warning | Radio Selection | Indicate if your level can cause any issues to people with Epilepsy | | Level Description | Text | Description for your level theme and gameplay style. Can be also used as a level introduction or crediting | | Level Tags | Text | Single word indicators to find your level. Separate each tag with commas | | Artist links | Text | URL info about the artist. Separate each URL with commas | | Speed Trial Multiplier Aim | Numerical | Sets the speed trial goal to your level | | Difficulty | Multiple Selection | 1 to 10 scoring on level difficulty | {% hint style="info" %} In case the music has a \*\*public license\*\*, or you are the artist, permission is \*\*not required\*\* on Proof of Artist's Permission {% endhint %} {% hint style="success" %} For better knowledge on how to \*\*score the difficulty\*\* of your level, go to \[Difficulty Scoring Methods\](/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/difficulty-scoring-methods.md) {% endhint %} {% hint style="success" %} To fully customize your Level Titles, go to \[Formatting Syles\](/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/formatting-styles.md) {% endhint %} {% hint style="warning" %} These Settings are \*\*necessary\*\* if you want to \*\*export levels\*\*. Go to \[Export and Publish Levels\](/english/know-the-basics/export-and-publish-levels.md) to know more {% endhint %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/FBjO7QTJNsg4k5C5LpId)

Editor - Level Settings Tab (Top)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/mXJfgK6XkviUQYRnrAWy)

Editor - Level Settings Tab (Bottom)

Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/locate-levels-files.md). # Locate levels files ## • Opening your most recent level {% hint style="warning" %} This will open your \*\*last viewed\*\* level in the editor, regardless of its creator. {% endhint %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/80EWJKAHLYggRzmCOBtU)

Editor Top Bar - Open "filename"

When you open the \*\*Top bar menu\*\*, you can access your most recent level. This will trigger a \*\*warning\*\* to ensure that your current level editing won't be lost by switching levels.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/msVBN362LMkgrrp2hzCk)

Editor - Opening a new level warning

You can now begin editing your most recent opened level!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/sty5eiML1h7aOavzKaeM)

Editor - Most recent level

\*\*\* ## • Opening a level saved on your computer Open the \*\*Top Bar Menu\*\*, and then select the \*\*Open...\*\* Option. This time, the game will open \*\*your computer explorer\*\*.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/vsiU042EXXGjgZSl6xD0)

Editor - Windows Explorer

Select the level you would like to open, and the editor will start loading everything for you! \*You might have to look for the folder where you typically storage your .adofai levels.\*

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/KmUm3JF9WTv64mhmDldf)

Editor - UFO level

\*\*\* ## • Opening a level with a URL **File Storage Websites** - _(Use these to storage your levels on the cloud)_ \* Discord -> \* Catbox -> \[https://catbox.moe\](https://catbox.moe/) \* MediaFire -> \### NOT RECOMMENDED \* Google Drive -> \[~~https://drive.google.com/~~\](https://drive.google.com/) \* Mega -> \[~~https://mega.nz/~~\](https://mega.nz/) \* OneDrive -> \[~~https://onedrive.live.com~~\](https://onedrive.live.com) \* Degoo -> \[~~https://degoo.com/~~\](https://degoo.com/) You can open .zip files from the web directly onto the editor. To do this, go to the \*\*Top Menu bar\*\*, select \*\*Open with URL...\*\*, and paste the URL from the storage website to download the file onto your computer. This will open the level immediately on the editor, ready to edit.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/mTBeEF8FF9cRufyZVazP)

Editor Top Bar - URL Level Download

{% hint style="warning" %} Opened Levels might not be compatible with your current game version. Always check your version and match it with the level file version to ensure everything works. {% endhint %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/TywtaUePxqAUPSXF6dc1)

Editor - URL level loaded

Audio file for your level music  
(_Accepts .ogg .mp3 .wav .aiff .aif extensions)_  
_(Ideal: .ogg)_

| | Beats per minute | Numerical | Starting speed of your level | | Volume | Numerical | % of volume your music will be played at start | | Offset | Numerical | Delay in milliseconds, added to your gameplay start so it matches the audio timing | | Pitch | Numerical |

Playback speed of the level in %  
_(100% = Original speed)_

| | Hitsound | Multiple selection | Sound each tile will play when hit | | Sound Volume | Numerical | % of volume each hitsound will be played | | Countdown ticks | Numerical | Number of beats in the countdown timer until the level's starting beat | {% hint style="info" %} To calculate your Beats per minute and Offset correctly, head over \[Finding the Correct BPM & Offset\](/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset.md). These are \*\*essential values\*\* for your level creation! {% endhint %}

# What Is Tech Charting? | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/introduction-to-tech-charts/what-is-tech-charting.md)
.

A Tech chart is one of the two most common types of charting, with the other type being Classic charting. While Classic charting revolves around having relatively simple gameplay, relying on concepts presented in the official levels, Tech charting goes beyond, having patterns where you would need to use two or more keys at once, being them at the same time or in a sequence of each other, and more complicated patterns. Tech charts can range from requiring medium skill levels to requiring skills that only the best of the best players have.

If this is your first time experimenting with a Tech Chart, here is a recommendation for you:

[![Logo](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fsteamcommunity.com%2Ffavicon.ico&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=41039212&sv=2)Steam Workshop::Tanger - Backyard Sanctuarysteam](https://steamcommunity.com/sharedfiles/filedetails/?id=2782132613)

[PreviousIntroduction To Tech Charts](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/introduction-to-tech-charts)
[NextCommon Characteristics / Patterns In Tech Charting](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/introduction-to-tech-charts/common-characteristics-patterns-in-tech-charting)

Last updated 2 years ago

---

# Smooth Pauses | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/smooth-pauses.md)
.

This practice is related to [Pause Tiles](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events/pause-tiles)
 Events

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/smooth-pauses#pause-indicators)

• Pause indicators


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Regarding pauses, these events are **not visible** to the player. So it is important to find creative ways to let the player know the pause tile exists, regardless of how long the pause is

#### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/smooth-pauses#using-gaps)

**Using Gaps**

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FZS17OWtFB5smvBCaeWBq%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De5bc30d0-6563-4b34-bc66-e2ede5fac49b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=84415eab&sv=2)

Pause - Using gaps and tile movement

#### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/smooth-pauses#using-colors)

**Using Colors**

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FRnA29I2Ac2e2foWTp4VR%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57e0376c-4991-4656-8d5d-f6001ecb6eff&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a79a594a&sv=2)

Pause - Color and Tile Format

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/smooth-pauses#pause-consistency)

• Pause consistency


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When it comes to using pauses, you have to take into consideration, these events are **not meant** to correct any offsets or adjust tile placement. So for this example, here's something you **shouldn't do**

Pause - Bad usage of pause tiles

To guarantee consistency, always use values that assure the beat doesn't create on-beat rotations. This is true for every angle the pause event is being active, 1 pause beat is always 180º no matter the tile angle:

180º -> 1 Pause Beat 90º -> 0.5 Beats 270º -> 1.5 Beats 360º -> 2 Beats

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FS9EIShuGjvPOyE8T6qUO%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69401deb-ffe0-4800-8700-c1b2c3847d4f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d21bc484&sv=2)

Pause - Rotation with angles

[NextRepeat Events Set-up](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/repeat-events-set-up)

# Tech Chart Playing Techniques | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/introduction-to-tech-charts/tech-chart-playing-techniques.md)
.

When play testing a Tech chart, you need to know how to play them, so here is a quick tutorial: To start, since the BPM is probably too high in order to only use one hand to play, you can try to use both by alternating the hand you are currently using repeatedly, demonstrated in the video below. For normal pseudos, you will need to use two keys at once, and for that, don't use both hands to hit two keys at once. Instead, hit two keys using the same hand, which is also demonstrated in the video below.

Teaching how to start alternating your hands into tech charts, Gameplay by Dirt 📝Backyard Sanctuary, composed by Tanger. Chart by Bocchi _(not the anime character)_

For faster BPMs, try to speed up your key presses following the same technique above.

Teaching how to press keys on fast tech charts, Gameplay by Dirt 📝Inferno, composed by F-777. Chart by ShinJW

For harder Tech charts, only 2 keys won't be enough. Because of that, a technique called **rolling** is used, where you alternate between 4 keys or more. This technique can have many variations on how you execute it, but in the video below, the rolling goes from the outer keys (middle fingers) to the inner keys (index fingers).

Showing 4 keys rolling for fast Magic shapes patterns, Gameplay by Dirt 📝The Limit Does Not Exist, composed by Cardboard Box. Chart by -K and BamgoeSN

[PreviousExamples Of Classic Vs Tech Charts](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/introduction-to-tech-charts/examples-of-classic-vs-tech-charts)
[NextWorkshop and Level Hunting](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/workshop-and-level-hunting)

Last updated 2 years ago

# Decoration and Text Creative Format | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format/color-and-alpha-styling)

![Cover](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F7PP09WAA7OE4YV32L32W%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f8e80da-c44a-4b7b-ba91-9ba9e7a6b88b&width=490&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=45dc3bda&sv=2)

# Other Shortcuts | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/other-shortcuts.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/other-shortcuts#list-of-shortcuts)

List of Shortcuts


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Keyboard Input

Description

`1~9`

[Adds a new instance of the event on the select tile](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/other-shortcuts/adds-a-new-instance-of-the-event-on-the-select-tile)

`A`

[Toggle autoplay](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/other-shortcuts/toggle-autoplay)

`N`

[Toggle no-fail](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/other-shortcuts/toggle-no-fail)

`Ctrl + H`

[Open/close the "Keyboard Shortcuts" Menu In-Game](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/other-shortcuts/open-close-the-keyboard-shortcuts-menu-in-game)

`Shift + F1`

[Show editor guidelines](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/other-shortcuts/show-editor-guidelines)

`Ctrl + Alt + L`

[Open the log directory](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/other-shortcuts/open-the-log-directory)

`Ctrl + F`

[Show tile numbers](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/other-shortcuts/show-tile-numbers)

`Ctrl + Shift + F`

[Show selected tile number](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/other-shortcuts/show-selected-tile-number)

_Click on each_ _Shortcut Description_ _for more information and video examples_

[PreviousExit Play mode at current tile](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/gameplay/exit-play-mode-at-current-tile)
[NextAdds a new instance of the event on the select tile](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/shortcuts-listing/other-shortcuts/adds-a-new-instance-of-the-event-on-the-select-tile)
