# Difficulty Scoring Methods | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/difficulty-scoring-methods.md)
.

These level suggestions do not offer any Tech Charts evaluation. These are merely for **Classic Levels**

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/difficulty-scoring-methods#how-to-score-your-level-in-difficulty-before-exporting-it)

How to score your level in difficulty before exporting it?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For an alternative to the in-game difficulty scoring system, check [adofai.gg](https://adofai.gg/)
, having more levels of difficulty scoring than 10

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/difficulty-scoring-methods#whats-1-gem)

• What's 1 Gem?

🔹 If your level includes/uses:

*   BPM goes up to 160
    
*   Angles under 90° don't exist
    
*   No more than 3 consecutive fast angles
    
*   Patterns are short and easy to read
    
*   Chart being completely visible across the level
    

🔺 If your level enforces:

*   Nothing
    

Then your Level is probably a **Level 1** gem difficulty

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FapPJmyuPIZtj00QPhFIE%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5fd8e92c-4dee-4e46-812d-be7e16c3d3a2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3e234219&sv=2)

Level 1

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/difficulty-scoring-methods#whats-2-gems)

• What's 2 Gems?

🔹 If your level includes/uses:

*   BPM goes up to 190
    
*   Angles under 45° don't exist
    
*   No more than 3 consecutive fast angles
    
*   Patterns are short and easy to read
    
*   Chart being completely visible across the level
    

🔺 If your level enforces:

*   Nothing
    

Then your Level is probably a **Level 2** gem difficulty

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FLXbFcljD2OKp7ZQ3dHIg%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb6e76a4-b5a2-454e-856a-28e22eb8e8a3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c009c408&sv=2)

Level 2

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/difficulty-scoring-methods#whats-3-gems)

• What's 3 Gems?

🔹 If your level includes/uses:

*   BPM goes up to 210
    
*   No more than 5 consecutive fast angles
    
*   Patterns are short and easy to read
    
*   Chart being completely visible across the level
    

🔺 If your level enforces:

*   Filters and/or Decorations that block visibility partially
    

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FONTse79BMGK1Iqxn2Xae%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D03a580e6-3769-42ff-9172-2aeedec0b591&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=77eaec3a&sv=2)

Level 3

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/difficulty-scoring-methods#whats-4-gems)

• What's 4 Gems?

🔹 If your level includes/uses:

*   BPM goes up to 240
    
*   No more than 9 consecutive fast angles
    
*   Patterns are a bit long but still easy to read
    
*   Chart being completely visible across the level
    

🔺 If your level enforces:

*   Filters and/or Decorations that block visibility partially
    

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FgNWX9M12NN5zvhhxkRRt%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e09f6fa-ad85-419f-a9e6-e465a898fd62&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c3a0a402&sv=2)

Level 4

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/difficulty-scoring-methods#whats-5-gems)

• What's 5 Gems?

🔹 If your level includes/uses:

*   BPM goes up to 270
    
*   Chart being occasionally less visible across the level
    
*   Patterns are a bit long but still easy to read
    

🔺 If your level enforces:

*   Filters and/or Decorations that block visibility partially
    
*   Mechanics that are somewhat difficult to play, but not difficult to understand
    

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FtzsBJfIboNksBzFF9LDE%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deb5e22fe-d374-47cf-bceb-04ea37c4407b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=15be37ea&sv=2)

Level 5

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/difficulty-scoring-methods#whats-6-gems)

• What's 6 Gems?

🔹 If your level includes/uses:

*   BPM goes up to 300
    
*   Chart being occasionally less visible across the level
    
*   Patterns are a bit long and a bit harder to read
    

🔺 If your level enforces:

*   Typical patterns charted differently, but not difficult to understand
    
*   Filters and/or Decorations that block visibility partially
    
*   Mechanics that are somewhat difficult to play, but not difficult to understand
    

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fs75NICM8o6ke1IsX6S1y%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da4ba482e-85f3-4b1d-869c-e1f9955cdb92&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94f96d92&sv=2)

Level 6

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/difficulty-scoring-methods#whats-7-gems)

• What's 7 Gems?

🔹 If your level includes/uses:

*   BPM goes up to 350
    
*   Chart being frequently less visible across the level
    
*   Patterns are a bit long and a bit harder to read
    

🔺 If your level enforces:

*   Typical patterns charted differently, but not difficult to understand
    
*   Filters and/or Decorations that block visibility massively
    
*   Mechanics that are hard to play, but not difficult to understand
    

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FNrqbTvdZowyeByStbqSH%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D010c3b95-096f-49f5-aee6-7b6fcf20e456&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9de3ddbb&sv=2)

Level 7

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/difficulty-scoring-methods#whats-8-gems)

• What's 8 Gems?

🔹 If your level includes/uses:

*   BPM goes up to 400
    
*   Chart being frequently less visible across the level
    
*   Patterns are quite big and hard to read
    

🔺 If your level enforces:

*   Typical patterns charted differently, but are somewhat hard to understand
    
*   Filters and/or Decorations that block visibility massively
    
*   Mechanics that are hard to play, but not difficult to understand
    

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FfRlqezSZnbfQuk0wYPHk%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0c006396-dacc-4e01-a158-807e84d52868&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=45e2384e&sv=2)

Level 8

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/difficulty-scoring-methods#whats-9-gems)

• What's 9 Gems?

🔹 If your level includes/uses:

*   BPM goes up to 450
    
*   Chart being hardly visible across the level
    
*   Patterns are quite big and hard to read
    

🔺 If your level enforces:

*   Typical patterns charted differently, but are somewhat hard to understand
    
*   Filters and/or Decorations that block visibility massively
    
*   Mechanics that are hard to play and understand
    

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FzPdjNqIWKChpI4JcmSut%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c6181ef-2a8c-4a11-b15c-b17efc308192&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc00e1c9&sv=2)

Level 9

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/difficulty-scoring-methods#whats-10-gems)

• What's 10 Gems?

🔹 If your level includes/uses:

*   BPM higher than 450
    
*   Chart being hardly visible across the level
    
*   Patterns are quite big and hard to read
    

🔺 If your level enforces:

*   Typical patterns charted differently, and are difficult to understand
    
*   Filters and/or Decorations that block visibility massively
    
*   Mechanics that are hard to play and understand
    

Then your Level is probably a **Level 10** gem difficulty

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FJz6lecoETG902v4JJFbb%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D959800a6-9f49-49f4-b00d-b9ce86160260&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=da075698&sv=2)

Level 10

[PreviousFormatting Styles](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/formatting-styles)
[NextEvent Skillful Formatting and Showcases](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases)

# Easing Showcase | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/easing-showcase.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/easing-showcase#list-of-eases)

List of Eases


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every video has a camera movement of **Y=1 / Y=-1** and tile movement **X=2**

_Check all easing function at_ [_https://easings.net_](https://easings.net/#)

# Filters Showcase | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/filters-showcase.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/filters-showcase#list-of-filters)

List of Filters


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every video includes both 100%, 0%, -100 % and a 100 to -100% transition intensity. The only exceptions to this rule are filters that have unique interactions on specific intensities (e.g. LED), along with filters that have no setting options (e.g. 80's TV).

# Common Characteristics / Patterns In Tech Charting | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/introduction-to-tech-charts/common-characteristics-patterns-in-tech-charting.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/introduction-to-tech-charts/common-characteristics-patterns-in-tech-charting#pseudos)

• Pseudos


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F508DR7LsR7gHoceOtZvK%252FPseudo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca6aa78d-be2f-4e50-b106-b57a6130f091&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f40aa631&sv=2)

_30° Pseudo_

Pseudos are basically double-hit patterns. They work similarly to the multi-hit tiles in World RJ, where you need to press two keys at once. These are the most common pattern in the entirety of Tech charts, as they elevate the difficulty of a level by a high amount. These are specifically hard-coded to work when multiple keys _(in this case, two)_ are pressed at the same time, as declared by some developers.

The pseudos in the picture above are made using 30° angles, which is the most common angle for pseudos at fast songs (300 BPM or above), but another angle that tends to be used frequently is 15°, for slower parts of songs (150 - 300 BPM) or for tighter hit windows. If a song is slower than 150 BPM, you can use smaller angle turns for pseudos using the insert custom angle option.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FA0Z9S4demnftdu1dkpCo%252F15pseudo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7362974f-d05c-450e-99af-46e1345eb06c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f0b66e4a&sv=2)

_15° Pseudo_

Interestingly, when twirls are used in the second tile of a pseudo, you can add tiles at a 60° angle in relation to the second tile of the pseudo and it will work. This happens because the angle distance between the planet on the previous tile and the next tile stays the same in this type of twirl, which involves On-Beat Rotation.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FzwUhY7QypXhGlNMBVy60%252F30Twirlpseudo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De690151b-2897-483f-acfe-250cc3826d88&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe391ffa&sv=2)

_30° Twirl Pseudo_

This is also valid for 15° pseudos, where instead of the next tiles being at 60° for it to work, they are at 30°.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FRXvr9hv6HWTlV9dFBZUt%252FCaptura%2520de%2520tela%25202023-06-28%2520230311.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4b4492f7-503b-4d99-884b-1dea94aa20c7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f73bd67f&sv=2)

_15° Twirl Pseudo_

Pseudos can be mixed with other shapes for more interesting gameplay. They can give some good variety to the level, and make it more dynamic, as well as, of course, making it harder as well.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F376jj9Jm10Htu5n4Dl6A%252FPseudoPatterns.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dde374c42-c553-4fd4-8cda-c47e67fc5b9f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f3c1f841&sv=2)

_(Angle for the pseudos at the hexagons:) (30°: 90° at the first pseudo, 30° at the second one) (15°: 105° at the first pseudo, 15° at the second one)_

You can also use more twirls on pseudos to create double-speed pseudos (_not final name_). These act like normal pseudos, but, as the name suggests, they need to be hit at double the current BPM of the level.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FzPXXeXRfVoqzi9nQm3to%252F30DoubleSpeedPseudo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5fb561ed-9f01-48f3-be75-2ccfd82d0d8b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8d4b401d&sv=2)

_30° 30° angle turn then 60° angle turn on repeat, with twirls_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F6DPYaywwOd4R50meBMLG%252F15DoubleSpeedPseudo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1132bfe1-e1d9-4767-a587-3e5d83a26d4e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=83ecc7ed&sv=2)

15° 15_° angle turn then 75° angle turn on repeat, with twirls_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FbfpxKSfyRKRZoGV7Dmvj%252F30DoubleSpeedPseudos2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbe1fab5b-c745-401b-9ec6-2dd167254291&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2d3c267&sv=2)

_30° When it turns itself by 90°, turn it by 60° without a twirl in the last tile to make it horizontal again_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FcLaiqQ5T8eNe6G6lXorA%252F15DoubleSpeedPseudos2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dafddcf1a-79e9-47e3-ab96-1f20f6e92143&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f62872a3&sv=2)

15° Turn it by 75° after 3 pseudos to have a full 360° turn

Pseudos, while they can just stay On-beat, they also can skip a beat if you use 330° for 30° pseudos, or 345° for 15° pseudos, similar to a 360° turn.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F1iz1yoatz9QK3X6pvoco%252F30-360pseudoAnd15-360pseudo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc8f12f1-d009-4638-81d1-63add25d53ec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fbed170&sv=2)

_30° Beat-skip pseudo (left) and 15° Beat-skip pseudo (right)_

The rule for the twirl on the second tile of the pseudo is also true here, while having an On-beat Rotation that adds up to 360°.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FZncV0Tw1N9Dm58z18xoa%252F30-360Twirlpseudo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D867e02ab-a2a8-4969-872d-d4df7f362cd4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ee215aa&sv=2)

_30° Twirl Beat-skip pseudos_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FobkpA4WSR4b0PZ1Zuu5t%252F15-360Twirlpseudo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9d4bdce3-d87b-45c1-b9a2-70016e26b950&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e140a667&sv=2)

_15° Twirl Beat-skip pseudos_

Mid-spins can also be used to create pseudos, and they have interesting interactions relating to On-beat Rotation.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FOaPjgrIoGedSLiQ7yv8f%252FMidspinPseudos.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D04e9aab4-f316-4ab9-9096-93496e15400c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ab18f2e1&sv=2)

_30° Mid-spin pseudo (Left) and 15° Mid-spin pseudo (Right)_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FvciBIlvW1VSrxCF8q0do%252F360MidspinPseudos.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da6d3c6b5-94a4-423c-8809-a2d25339484d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f6be7e04&sv=2)

_30° Mid-spin Beat-skip pseudo (Right) and 15° Mid-spin Beat-Skip pseudo (Left)_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FAbtEszT0GmKdKOecaGQR%252F30TwirlMidspinpseudos.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0e70dad2-ea9b-41ec-a505-47a68b7940a8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6691a017&sv=2)

_30° Mid-spin Pseudos_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FVSKho04lf2DcXTBtqQUW%252F15Twirlmidspinpseudos.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14ffbbac-a931-4e76-bb37-e173a166a986&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2d7ff917&sv=2)

15_° Mid-spin Pseudos_

Another commonly used type of pseudo are the triple pseudos, which requires 3 keys to be hit. These are normally used at the 4th beat of a 4/4 song, but there's no general rule on where you should use these. Quadruple pseudos can also be used, which require 4 keys at once to hit, but are not as common as the ones listed before, and are not hard-coded to be hit correctly when pressing all the keys at the same time, unlike the previous patterns.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FCWo2qLAKhyHGcFNLJVTJ%252F3kPseudoAnd4kPseudo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D92970ecf-6bdc-4eaa-bbfd-d2dd8f8899ac&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9232d441&sv=2)

_30° Triple pseudo (Left) and 30° Quadruple pseudo (Right)_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FHE3fXvUlEdgkFOzeMbbE%252F15-3kPseudoAnd4kPseudo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D270dd349-0b14-4b4b-ad43-3baa6f92c1a5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fb3e2138&sv=2)

_15° Triple pseudo (Left) and 15° Quadruple pseudo (Right)_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F0fmb2CFY4Qx7ySxfDXcP%252F30Twirl-3kPseudoAnd4kPseudo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e2db94f-ed0a-4dcb-8a6e-cd3b37cd74e6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=13ecbfc1&sv=2)

_30° Twirl Triple pseudo (Bottom, 120° for the next tile to stay On-beat) and 30° Twirl Quadruple pseudo (Top, 90° for the next tile to stay On-beat)_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FhngYkc0qkyVaLNwhzItB%252F15Twirl-3kPseudoAnd4kPseudo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db01424ba-bf97-4784-98b2-e70f0df31446&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=984700b8&sv=2)

_15° Twirl Triple pseudo (Bottom, 150° for the next tile to stay On-beat) and 15° Twirl Quadruple pseudo (Top, 135° for the next tile to stay On-beat)_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FAhP9NE813MmgmrlY1DZ1%252F360-3-4kpseudo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De48cede5-4ad2-4ec5-9333-8f72ba9553f8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c59f8949&sv=2)

_30° Twirl Beat-skip Triple pseudo_ _(Right, 300° for the next tile to stay On-beat) and 30° Twirl Beat-skip Quadruple pseudo (Left, -90° for the next tile to stay On-beat)_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FV7dZudo2rISVYeGfdOMM%252F15-360-3-4kpseudos.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D214658a4-d4ff-4222-b830-7bd2c6c94260&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d75c2597&sv=2)

_30° Twirl Beat-skip Triple pseudo_ _(Right, 330° for the next tile to stay On-beat) and 30° Twirl Beat-skip Quadruple pseudo (Left, 315° for the next tile to stay On-beat)_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fhlnw8XnDFAqMD4PYkFio%252F30-360Twirl3-4kpseudo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D12054867-738a-44e1-823e-6df44692516b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=980e7fc0&sv=2)

_30° Twirl Beat-skip Triple pseudo_ _(Bottom, -60° for the next tile to stay On-beat) and 30° Twirl Beat-skip Quadruple pseudo (Top, -105° for the next tile to stay On-beat)_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F8HpXgz1brqhcRnKdmvNK%252F15-360Twirl3-4kpseudos.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc16d80c1-7f06-48a2-bff8-33e9e8174d34&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=21a7c194&sv=2)

_15° Twirl Beat-skip Triple pseudo_ _(Bottom, 315° for the next tile to stay On-beat) and 15° Twirl Beat-skip Quadruple pseudo (Top, 300° for the next tile to stay On-beat)_

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/introduction-to-tech-charts/common-characteristics-patterns-in-tech-charting#zips)

• Zips


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Although not exactly a common trait only in Tech charting, zips are fairly more used here than in classic charting. Zips consist of a really basic pattern, where you use the same angle repeatedly for the next tile, using twirls on all of them. The most common types are from the base angles provided by the editor itself (I.e. the tile key shortcuts).

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FkDOvcurAvcFpplb5ljUZ%252FZips.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D02b34766-911f-4b4f-8d71-6c9e674a6801&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56fffce2&sv=2)

_90° 5 tile zip (1), 75° 5 tile zip (2), 60° 5 tile zip (3), 45° 5 tile zip (4), 30° 5 tile zip (5) and 15° 5 tile zip (6)_

These, most of the time, are already enough for a regular Tech chart. Note that you can extend these for as much as you want.

[PreviousWhat Is Tech Charting?](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/introduction-to-tech-charts/what-is-tech-charting)
[NextExamples Of Classic Vs Tech Charts](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/introduction-to-tech-charts/examples-of-classic-vs-tech-charts)

Last updated 2 years ago

# Magic Shapes | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/magic-shapes.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/magic-shapes#what-are-magic-shapes)

What are magic shapes?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Magic Shapes are very interesting when charting, where it consists of a pattern that is artificially changed to be played like an On-beat 180° straight line of a certain BPM using BPM multiplier events; which vary according to the song and pattern used. It's usually used when a song has a part where it's staying in the same rhythm for a long period of time, so they are used instead of normal straight lines to make gameplay more exciting, despite not necessarily changing it.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fd5E1OxtXDyZwFxuDC5Fq%252Fmpp1lastmagicshape.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3738a011-a32a-4b79-bbc2-3b34b6fab017&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5a408c98&sv=2)

📝_Plum - Mad Piano Party. Chart by Strode Example of a Magic Shape_

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/magic-shapes#how-to-create-magic-shapes)

How to create magic shapes?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

While for creating the shape itself, it doesn't require an specific method, it's only limited to your imagination. However, when making the angle turns, you will need to make sure that the BPM will always be the same throughout the entirety of the magic shape.

To calculate the value which will be used to multiply the BPM by, take the angle you will use next for the pattern and divide it by 180, then for the next multiplier, do the same thing but divide the value you got by the previous value you used for the previous BPM multiplier. As you use more and more BPM multipliers, for the next value, you will need to use more and more divide operations, including all the previous multiplier values you used, so as an alternative, you can use set BPM to make it easier to process, by just dividing the angle used by 180, and then multiplying the original BPM of the song by the value you acquired, and using that value as next BPM change. For example, supposing that a magic shape is being created for a chart with 300 BPM, and a 45° angle turn is used, the calculation `45/180` is made, to find the value for the BPM multiplier, which is equal to `0.25`, and if a 135° angle turn is used next, the calculation `(135/180)/0.25` is made, to find the value for the next BPM multiplier, which is based on the previously used value, bringing us to `3`. If a 90° angle turn is used, the calculation `(90/180)/3/0.5`, to find the next value, and so on. As an alternative method, the calculations `300x(45/180)`, `300x(135/180)` and `300x(90/180)` can be used to find the BPM for the angle turns respectively.

[PreviousFreezing Effects](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/freezing-effects)
[NextIntroduction To Tech Charts](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/introduction-to-tech-charts)

Last updated 2 years ago

*   [What are magic shapes?](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/magic-shapes#what-are-magic-shapes)
    
*   [How to create magic shapes?](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/magic-shapes#how-to-create-magic-shapes)

# Formatting Styles | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/formatting-styles.md)
.

The Editor is ready to accept customization qualities into any text you write. That even includes parameter values with text, like the Artist & Song.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/formatting-styles#editor-formatting-styles)

Editor formatting styles


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here are the elements available when customizing your texts:

*   **Bold** ⇾ `<b>yourtext</b>`
    

_The bold element brings a strong tone to your texts._

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FxcAkigRWk0OOVudhI54H%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8e3d3247-7b47-4212-8b52-7f6c3a1ace1f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=418cd7ce&sv=2)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FwiPdBxoip6lMU1PnBmVR%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D102f1f84-d25b-4f20-b92a-28d878454ad9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b6e50dd6&sv=2)

* * *

*   _Italic_ ⇾ `<i>yourtext</i>`
    

_The italic element slight inclines your texts to the side._

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F86vFslG7ku6KSBCu63b9%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3fb879dc-fc6f-4dd8-b3b0-36fb3d1c340e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b600bff2&sv=2)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FSB7KqiDEVoGpWopRLj7s%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6eb793d-021f-481f-a2ab-472a40bfecb9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1b672c93&sv=2)

* * *

*   Color ⇾ `<color=red>yourtext</color>` or `<color=004400>yourtext</color>`
    

_The color element gives some tint into your texts. It can also play with the hue of colors._

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FqEYW5NY9vYRJJNdP41jr%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De5d1b0da-7cd5-465b-b8fb-e433fb004c1a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f8d28a56&sv=2)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FpVnIEzCF6b72gaUPfJmS%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0cef5a4b-63e9-44bb-a09c-0c932e169c4d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ec54fc7d&sv=2)

Video

Event Settings

Info

Event Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Ease

Multiple Selection

Sets the easing movement for the planets rotation animation

Ease parts

Numerical

Sets how many times the planets create the ease movement selected, every 360º _(180º = one beat)_

Ease part behavior

Radio Selection

Select the way the planets imitate the ease movement on each part _(Repeat = same ease / Mirror = opposite ease)_

_You can check all easing behavior on the_ _Event Skillful Formatting and Showcases -_ [_Easing Showcase_](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/easing-showcase)

# Under / Over Charting | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/under-over-charting.md)
.

This practice is related to [Tile Placement](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement)
 and [Gameplay](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events)
 Events

A song can be charted in any way you would like, but that doesn't mean it will always be good. When charting a song incorrectly, one of two cases can happen: **Under** Charting, or **Over** Charting.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/under-over-charting#under-charting)

• Under Charting


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A chart is classified as Under Charted when it syncs to the song, but the chart takes so few elements of the song, that it either feels like it could fit for any other song, due to how overly plain it is, or it just ends up being boring gameplay.

Example of a Bad way of Undercharting

While Under Charting can lead up to the problems mentioned above, you can in fact make a good chart while not charting all/most elements of the song. To do that, charting the powerful notes of a song is the key. For instance, on the 4/4 song, the 1st and the 3rd note are the powerful ones. **1** 2 **3** 4, **1** 2 **3** 4. However, **that doesn't mean you should not chart some of the weak notes**, as doing some improvising with them can lead up to some interesting gameplay, instead of only charting the powerful notes, which will definitely lead up to boring gameplay.

Example of a Good way of Undercharting

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/under-over-charting#over-charting)

• Over Charting


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A chart is classified as Over Charted when while it follows the song, it also charts elements that are not really in the song, but although if done in a good way, that actually enhances the gameplay, it can also lead up to a chart that doesn't feel like it was even trying to sync with the song at all.

Example of a Bad way of Overcharting

But that doesn't mean there are no cases where charting elements that are not present in a song is a good thing, and it can be if done right. To do so, just make sure to be following how the song sounds, and that whatever you may end up adding to the chart that is not a present element in the song fits. This is mostly the case for **Tech charts**, where it is basically one of its core elements.

Example of a Good way of Overcharting

To learn more about **Tech charts**, check [Introduction To Tech Charts](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/introduction-to-tech-charts)
.

[PreviousBPM Speeds](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/bpm-speeds)
[NextHidden Twirls and On-beat rotation](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/hidden-twirls-and-on-beat-rotation)

Last updated 2 years ago

*   [• Under Charting](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/under-over-charting#under-charting)
    
*   [• Over Charting](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/under-over-charting#over-charting)

---

# Editor Comment | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/conveniences/editor-comment.md)
.

This event can stack multiple instances on the same tile

Video

Event Settings

Info

Event Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Comment

Text _HTML inspired format_

Simple commentary area for the editor only

_Text format used is_ _**Unity's Rich Text**__, which is based on the working tags of HTML formalization_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FwtXlkLsnbwYLRQ3kgKS8%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2618523d-6c01-4983-af56-5a57f238f10b&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dab76b5&sv=2)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F6ecHiTquvhl1VoSdCPfk%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9d95a2b9-7480-4fd5-8825-35e908e9e12b&width=73&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=74c5e4a5&sv=2) -> Editor Comment Icon

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/conveniences/editor-comment#editor-formatting-styles)

Editor formatting styles

*   **Bold** \-> `<b>yourtext</b>`
    
*   _Italic_ \-> `<i>yourtext</i>`
    
*   Color -> `<color=red>yourtext</color>` or `<color=004400>yourtext</color>`
    
*   Size -> `<size=100>yourtext</size>`
    

_As of the moment, there are several tags aside these, but they were_ _not implemented_ _to work in this event_

Formats must be closed from the **last** to the **first** one used

**Purple Icons** can only be seen on the editing side. During gameplay, they disappear but work as the same

[PreviousConveniences](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/conveniences)
[NextBookmark](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/conveniences/bookmark)

Last updated 2 years ago

# Recolor Track | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/track-events/recolor-track.md)
.

This event can stack multiple instances on the same tile

Video

Event Settings

Info

Event Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Start tile

Numerical with Multiple Selection _Accepts both integers_

The first tile this event will affect

End tile

Numerical with Multiple Selection _Accepts both integers_

The last tile this event will affect

Gap length

Numerical

Gap between tiles that will be affected by the event

Track color type

Multiple Selection

Type of pattern /animation the tiles will present

Track color

Hex Code

Changes the color of the tiles

Track style

Multiple Selection

Sets the style of the tiles

Glow intesity

Numerical

Intenstity of the glow that appears on a tile after being hit

Angle offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Used to set the start delay of the event, in degrees _(0º = on hit)_

Event tag

Text

Sets a tag that indentifies this event to other events. Can be used for repetition or easy event set-ups

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FtmA22tYUke914UfnUkaf%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df66d638b-0f33-4c2e-9853-03976aa6fc12&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=170aaed2&sv=2)

# Move Track | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/track-events/move-track.md)
.

This event can stack multiple instances on the same tile

Video

Event Settings

Info

Event Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Start tile

Numerical with Multiple Selection _Accepts both integers_

The first tile this event will affect

End tile

Numerical with Multiple Selection _Accepts both integers_

The last tile this event will affect

Gap length

Numerical

Gap between tiles that will be affected by the event

Duration

Numerical

The amount of beats the animation will last

Position offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

How offset the tiles will place compared to the original event tile position. _Works on X and Y axis_

Rotation offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

How much the tile will rotate, compared to its last rotation value

Scale

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Indicates which size the tile will be

Opacity

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Changes how transparent the event tile gets

Angle offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Value in degress used to set the start delay of this event _(0º = on hit)_

Ease

Multiple Selection

Sets which easing is used for the transition animation of this event

Event tag

Text

Sets a tag that indentifies this event to other events. Can be used for repetition or easy event set-ups

_You can check all easing behavior on the_ _Event Skillful Formatting and Showcases -_ [_Easing Showcase_](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/easing-showcase)
 _section._

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FJ95cnBuynb7Mp8OjGjXh%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D02f60660-60cb-4554-b02e-9bd8f76b6d00&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ac55d69a&sv=2)

# Elevator Tracks | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/elevator-tracks.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/elevator-tracks#what-are-elevators)

What are elevators?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Elevators are tiles that move with the level up and down when they are hit. A good example of this gimmick being played is on the official world XT, where the colored tiles represent the elevators going up.

📝World XT - Options, video by Nichipe

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/elevator-tracks#how-to-create-an-elevator-tile)

How to create an elevator tile?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Elevator tiles have no limitation to the kind of angle we insert to allow this gimmick to be consistent. For this example, we only use U-turns representing 360º angle tiles or 2 beats.

Starting on, we create the track, taking into consideration which tiles will be moving up or down, moving the next ones on the track, higher or lower of the original position with the [Position Track](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/track-events/position-track)
 Event

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fyrfdsos41yy81DgUPD7L%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd2960e2e-84b3-4251-8a45-82ff19d20283&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=590ccc2f&sv=2)

Editor - Position track on tile after the U-turn

After setting all tracks to their position, let's follow the style, so we can better represent our elevator tiles

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FXsJM7GrI7TqhurCJf2Il%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8a5913ec-a19b-4dc7-b9bb-aa62e9d9daf9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cc06d079&sv=2)

Editor - Coloring the track to help elevators

Using a [Set Track Color](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/track-events/set-track-color)
 Event, color the tiles to use as the elevator. Color is up to your level theme and preference. Make sure to do the same on the tiles you don't want to return to the track's original color.

There are other ways to color tracks during gameplay, however, they involve angle offset, so they are harder to set up. Feel free to explore alternative ways while experimenting with the editor!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FiZpfCEaCZYbJWpUMtm9W%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db0b33369-2029-493f-beb0-55f62f984a73&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4b1d249d&sv=2)

Editor - Coloring the elevator tiles

The track is now fully prepared to start the elevator tiles

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FwcExjDM13449Z67DEYho%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D017b2045-157e-41da-89d2-d139dd027df4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=27fd44b6&sv=2)

Editor - Track ready to move tiles with each elevator color

On the U-turn tiles, add a [Move Track](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/track-events/move-track)
 Event that only affects itself (Start tile & End tile = 0), next follow that up with a duration under the tile beat (in this case, U-turn take 2 beats, so we can use 1 beat as the duration of the elevator), and set the new position to be the same height as the following track, as set when using the Position Track Events

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Faqu32CTWOWy3yGuODcEl%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D08e27449-f18f-46f9-b786-8fefb4b4aacd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=40273b9&sv=2)

Editor - Preparing the tile to move up as elevators on hit

Do this for every tile you want to create the elevator gimmick at

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FMXqqA8weGtVb2Q3NIfW0%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69e295d8-887f-4a24-be92-88cdc6624ded&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=20948e77&sv=2)

Editor - Elevator gimmick ready to play

Congratulations, you have now a level with elevator tiles on it!

[PreviousMulti-presses](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/multi-presses)
[NextFreezing Effects](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/freezing-effects)

Last updated 2 years ago

*   [What are elevators?](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/elevator-tracks#what-are-elevators)

# Set Hitsound | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events/set-hitsound.md)
.

This event cannot stack multiple instances on the same tile

Video

Event Settings

Info

Event Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Game Sound

Radio Selection

Sets the following hitsounds for every tile of the same type selected. _Midspins or Regular hits_

Hitsound

Multiple Selection

Sets the hitsound audio for the following tiles

Sound Volume

Numerical

Sets the volume of the following tiles hit

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FBwBos93PcoL4Oe3l1ccp%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6df2230-b472-46fc-bd71-2f2f129d860c&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4509af0d&sv=2)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FHqqPqCtj8mDrAqJLk9KO%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ae43d9f-3564-467d-a92d-6dbd4ad4a521&width=74&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5e258d9c&sv=2) -> Hit sound icon

**Purple Icons** can only be seen on the editing side. During gameplay, they disappear but work as the same

[NextPlay Sound](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events/play-sound)

# Repeat Events Set-up | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/repeat-events-set-up.md)
.

This practice is related to [Repeat](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/event-modifiers/repeat-events)
 Events

Creating events that can repeat themselves is possible with the repeat event. Its setup consists in 3 settings: **Repetitions**, **Interval,** and **Target tag**

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FVi1ahuVQSOgfoW5MD4zp%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df672f1f6-c813-4f1a-814d-d9436fd2d3ab&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4ef23ea7&sv=2)

Repeat Event - Settings

_Check more about_ [_Repeat Events_](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/event-modifiers/repeat-events)
 _on the_ _Events_ _Page_

The way repetition works will be to always follow the same actions as an existing event. That same effect has to be **set on the same tile** as the repeat event, or it won't work!

Here is the following example:

For this repeat, let's make the tiles rotate back and forward each beat. For that, let's set the events to Move Tracks and do each action (back, forward) on the editor

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F3HqtYcuGQb7kouVugfPk%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D60a0a8ca-9310-4585-8d8c-0c30a44e124a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aa9f059d&sv=2)

Move Tracks - 2 Events to move the whole track

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FRSRIYInb6SHdxVV8tbDH%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45f36012-f0d0-4894-abc1-a3d1b8d58c64&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=af5e9507&sv=2)

Move Tracks - Event 1 rotates clockwise and has tag "move1"

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FuXruL2Y2yUugQCLQjNRV%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D543e78fc-4c14-4ec8-86af-ee3a886321bd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c6b93ce0&sv=2)

Move Tracks - Event 2 rotates counter - clockwise and has tag "move2"

Now with both events ready and both with their unique tags, let's add a repeat event **on the same tile.** We want these events to repeat 3 times after the original move track and for each repeat to take 2 beats in between sets

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FiC0efdUnac7p7H5dblYG%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbbacfcbf-3cdf-4593-86f8-35ddcfd65f5d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8110af49&sv=2)

Repeat Events - Setting up 3 repetitions happening every 2 beats

Notice how the chart is pretty much empty, no events aside from the repeat and the move tracks are present on this chart. See the video to see the final effect come to live

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FmAuXewPOTmhkL9RAax5x%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Defb6b902-c0ba-481b-8a8e-7de0584b90b4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=69c19166&sv=2)

Editor - Testing the Repeat Event

[PreviousSmooth Pauses](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/smooth-pauses)
[NextConditional Events Prep](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/conditional-events-prep)

Last updated 2 years ago

# Text Decorations | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format/text-decorations.md)
.

Text Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Text

Text

Text that the current text will show

Font

Multiple Selection

Style you want your text to show

Position

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Set the text's position _Works on X and Y axis_

Relative to

Multiple Selection

Set from each POV you want your text to work with

Pivot offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Alters the pivot of the text, changing its center point

Rotation

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Set the text rotation angle

Lock Rotation

Radio Selection

Select if you want your text to rotate with your camera rotation

Scale

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Indicates which size the text will be

Lock Scale

Radio Selection

Select if you want your text to scale with your camera zoom

Color

Hex Code

Changes the base color of the text

Opacity

Numerical

Changes how transparent the text gets

Depth

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Place the text on virtual layers of depth to create the illusion of distance

Parallax

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Changes the travel distance of the text from the camera's POV _Works on X and Y axis_

Parallax offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Changes the starting position of the decor's travel distance from the camera's POV _Works on X and Y axis_

Tag

Text

Sets a tag that indentifies this text. _Can be used on events_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F6IV8G3JI3uTNecpWLRUX%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57a1caa1-6cec-4c05-b563-8f00ee885da6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3727f238&sv=2)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FVicxoFWAvccgPlCrC58U%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D62276ecf-c6bd-4739-8162-1437b95e684c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cdbd8736&sv=2)

[PreviousImage Decorations](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format/image-decorations)
[NextObject Decorations](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format/object-decorations)

# Set Speed | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events/set-speed.md)
.

This event can stack multiple instances on the same tile

Video

Event Settings

Info

Event Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Speed Type

Radio Selection

Indicates which speed type value is currently being used to make the speed change

Beats per Minute

Numerical

Value in BPM that sets the speed

BPM Multiplier

Numerical

Value Multiplier that multiplies this value to the current speed

Angle Offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Used to set the start delay of the event, in degrees _(0º = on hit)_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fi5DjXfkoZZxte8Ob3a12%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbae1c5ec-f50a-4eee-87b8-1fe669c60337&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6ae6106&sv=2)![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FSwxdlPK6A3FJx2PKveAo%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2164e9f6-a8a6-4154-bcd4-62bb19bb4ba8&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd2fe425&sv=2)![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FVfxPneDvHleg7Zp6iEod%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da584513f-6578-4de0-94b0-879d148b0fc5&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=87c46ec4&sv=2)![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FrdFdHbeHAf8OHRzN1e1I%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D998d7a61-8608-4992-a369-b78907d0d776&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=99df6549&sv=2)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F09pimZOaQgT33nWQC39C%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07a80238-3b66-4d5c-bbe4-da41005fd620&width=49&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e4c92084&sv=2) -> Snail

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FEYc52tnmOEJ5EKky29i1%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dec134f1d-f127-404e-b284-5ae0a306e549&width=51&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3a83c9d2&sv=2) -> Double Snail

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FYWQbEJ8A40iVX3jWt9Rj%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dccfc1b34-046b-4745-b146-5415eaf8c1d7&width=49&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=872a6a22&sv=2) -> Rabbit

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FA7plSGUMTUnA86HBFivB%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3fa59d7-5173-4275-9591-270e35adbfe1&width=54&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3099960d&sv=2) -> Double Rabbit

_Both the Snail/Rabbit indicate a speed below/above 5% of the current speed_

_Both the Double Snail/Rabbit indicate a speed below/above 205% the current speed_

The best practice for both these cases, is to only change the speed of the current BPM to half/double. In the Double Snail/Rabbit cases, to 4x times the current speed down/up.

_ie: 150 bpm -> 75 bpm (Half), 150 bpm -> 300 bpm (double)_

_Learn all good practices of_ _Set Speed_ _on the_ _Good practices_ _-_ [_BPM Speeds_](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/bpm-speeds)
 _section_

_Learn some cool gimmicks using this event on the_ _General Gimmicks_ _-_ [_Magic Shapes_](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/magic-shapes)
 _section_

[PreviousGameplay Events](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events)
[NextTwirl](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events/twirl)

Last updated 1 year ago

Info

Event Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Radio Selection

Enables/disables the hold start sound

Radio Selection

Enables/disables the hold loop sound

Hold end sound

Radio Selection

Enables/disables the hold end sound

Hold mid sound

Multiple Selection

Radio Selection

Numerical

Radio Selection

Numerical

# Hidden Twirls and On-beat rotation | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/hidden-twirls-and-on-beat-rotation.md)
.

This practice is related to [Twirl](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events/twirl)
 Events

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/hidden-twirls-and-on-beat-rotation#hidden-twirls)

• Hidden Twirls


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Twirls, when placed on bad spots in a level, can cause the gameplay to be impossible to read, as it may be covered by the track itself, making it hard/impossible for the player to know what to do next.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FItilZ9hJ1ezgXqoNZYIg%252FCaptura%2520de%2520tela%25202023-06-29%2520003600.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc721febf-9e0f-462a-ac84-1f9d21f45d13&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=379b3dff&sv=2)

_Twirl hidden behind a 90° turn tile_

In cases like these, it's better to move the twirl somewhere it's visible, while not affecting the gameplay itself in any way. But if that's not possible _(In this case, for demonstration purposes)_, Position Track events can always be used in order to fix this issue.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FEDYdo8bRAIkiwLR6J0lc%252FCaptura%2520de%2520tela%25202023-06-29%2520003724.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d47a4e2-7342-4601-bc62-eb3da61601c9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4788c9ae&sv=2)

_Twirl moved to the next tile on the track_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FRMTIMzXkLZ8Fkgh4hu31%252FCaptura%2520de%2520tela%25202023-06-29%2520003636.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfede188c-f7d1-4911-a0f6-8faf8911d3f3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9f287feb&sv=2)

_Position Track events making the twirl be visible without changing the tile it is at_

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/hidden-twirls-and-on-beat-rotation#on-beat-rotation)

• On-Beat Rotation


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On-Beat Rotation is when the angle turns don't add up to 180° or 360°, which represents the On-Beat of the song, and because of that, the sum of the angles, becomes the On-Beat of the song, despite not being 180° or 360°.

_On-Beat Rotation Example_

In the first pattern, the angles add up to 360°, avoiding On-Beat Rotation. `90+45+45+90+90=360°`

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FIbT4RZAEkJRBua4piY3w%252FCaptura%2520de%2520tela%25202023-06-28%2520003024.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deff74b83-6c71-40ec-8e3e-651c20fdb06c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c6adfc07&sv=2)

_Calculation made to find the current rotation of the track after the first pattern_

In the second pattern, the angles add up to -90°, causing On-Beat Rotation. Each time a twirl is used, the current operation is reversed. For example, in the image below, a twirl is used at the 45° turn, thus `-45`, and is used again for the next 45° turn, thus `+45`. `90-45+45-90-90=-90°`

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F0nPdHaxiWA2gS1mFCo2y%252FCaptura%2520de%2520tela%25202023-06-28%2520214924.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D205f19a9-26f8-4249-8734-6117bc95a7e9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1dbd2a2e&sv=2)

_Calculation made to find the current rotation of the track after the second pattern_

This can be used well if you know what you can with it, but **to avoid it, the easiest way would be to only use twirls when there's an angle distance of 90°, 180°, 270° and 360° from the starting angle**. Of course, On-Beat Rotation is not always guaranteed to happen when twirls are used on non-cardinal angles, but beware of where you place them, so it doesn't happen unintentionally.

[PreviousUnder / Over Charting](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/under-over-charting)
[NextSmooth Pauses](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/smooth-pauses)

Last updated 2 years ago

*   [• Hidden Twirls](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/hidden-twirls-and-on-beat-rotation#hidden-twirls)
    
*   [• On-Beat Rotation](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/hidden-twirls-and-on-beat-rotation#on-beat-rotation)

Type Validation

How offset the tiles will place compared to the original event tile position. _Works on X and Y axis_

Numerical with Multiple Selection _Accepts both integers_

Decides on which tile to start your event tile offset

Rotation

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Rotates the event tile and all following ones

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Scales the event tile and all following ones

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Changes how transparent the event tile and all following ones get

Only change this tile

Radio Selection

If enabled, all settings from this event will only affect the event tile

Editor only

# Freezing Effects | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/freezing-effects.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/freezing-effects#what-is-a-freezing-effect)

What is a freezing effect?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A freezing effect is when the screen appears to have frozen, or the game crashed, but it's actually just simulated making usage of visual effects, like the [Hall Of Mirrors](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/hall-of-mirrors)
 event.

📝Vista, composed by Inverted Silence. Chart and video by Econ, VFX by YeetYote

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/freezing-effects#how-to-create-a-freezing-effect)

How to create a freezing effect?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Remember to disable the tutorial background pattern, otherwise, the effect will break.

While the effect may look tricky and not easily doable at first glance, it actually requires a minimum of **6** events.

On the tile where the freeze will happen, put a [Move Camera](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/move-camera)
 event that will offset the camera by a high amount in the x or y-axis _(In this case 99, but do more if needed)_ with a **duration of 0 beats**. The other aspects of it, like what will it be relative to, are up to you. Then, with a [Hall Of Mirrors](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/hall-of-mirrors)
 event, **set to enabled**; along with a [Set Background](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/set-background)
 event, you will normally not need to change any of its settings.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FHTEPV9Gl1ZdLlaOZxxlo%252FCaptura%2520de%2520tela%25202023-07-10%2520035734.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa26fc7b-3161-4b8d-859f-1ef9a34418d2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=25c80541&sv=2)

Move Camera event settings - Starting tile

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FkUzUnZHNhTh80IAejmWA%252FCaptura%2520de%2520tela%25202023-07-10%2520035748.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D78a73b6a-fbb5-419e-bf1c-1056d53ef172&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=db3e2145&sv=2)

Hall Of Mirrors event settings - Starting tile

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FIkJib9EKemS8JICtj8tF%252FSetBackGroundFreeze.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91fff886-bab4-4d47-9d4f-67beb7489a86&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bbde2659&sv=2)

Set Background event settings - Starting tile

At the ending tile of the freeze, use the same events, but for the [Move Camera](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/move-camera)
 event, change the x/y-axis to its original value, disable the [Hall Of Mirrors](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/hall-of-mirrors)
 effect, and for the [Set Background](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/set-background)
 event, select the background image file _(if there is one)_ and set to its original values.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F54970XRAuWFVYP9XiikU%252FMoveCameraUnfreeze.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddf9f649a-61e7-43a5-8e00-27a981bf568f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5504546c&sv=2)

Move Camera event settings - Ending tile

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FaODs5thoEucxuxu87I8v%252FHOMUnfreeze.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6874c76-320d-47bb-8dca-e314e534cf6e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=32a6d911&sv=2)

Hall Of Mirrors event settings - Ending tile

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FTmPKVZOU6mCoqQHDDRNw%252FSetBackgroundUnfreeze.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1de9b7b0-c8d8-4fb2-ae62-22ae4f022e9b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dace4398&sv=2)

Set Background event settings - Ending tile

After doing that, you will have the base for a freeze effect. Now, it mostly depends on what visual effects you want to use to complement this one.

Here is another example where a freezing effect is used, based on what was taught here. Now, go make some good use of it!

[PreviousElevator Tracks](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/elevator-tracks)
[NextMagic Shapes](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/magic-shapes)

Last updated 2 years ago

*   [What is a freezing effect?](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/freezing-effects#what-is-a-freezing-effect)
    
*   [How to create a freezing effect?](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/freezing-effects#how-to-create-a-freezing-effect)
