# BPM Speeds | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/bpm-speeds.md)
.

This practice is related to [Set Speed](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/gameplay-events/set-speed)
 Events

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/bpm-speeds#hidden-speeds)

• Hidden Speeds


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F2t8stQlSi8k1qsvGHHxO%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df64607c7-2e31-46aa-9800-897d0eece0a1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c14d11f9&sv=2)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fp00htwpvsfH1dowpvvXo%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D137fad4e-f1da-4a73-9646-2d1cd0804cc3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bf829726&sv=2)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FIsjuE17z2b2XJim2DOpz%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2584d718-b89c-444f-8920-7bcc9d4df325&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1809a552&sv=2)

These should never be on the same tile together

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/bpm-speeds#ways-around-this-rule)

Ways around this rule

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/bpm-speeds#greater-than-bpm-building)

\-> **BPM building**

These builds, as long as previously informed, allow the player to take a guess on what the following tiles should be played

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FJ4A8AKk7kOrWJ6Rgrh1f%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De9df7464-b939-45eb-b434-343aaadc8be8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bd2d0af1&sv=2)

Example - BPM Build up scenario for hidden speeds

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/bpm-speeds#false-speed-changes)

• False speed changes


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FP2k2wCmmIGuYChhGOinw%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D468ddaf7-8a4a-4707-95a7-4fed3dcd822b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d4ed9f1f&sv=2)

Example - Speed random value

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F3rQnFa7s14J7fuDUNVw0%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D34d09b5d-60bd-46de-8a47-c297dea8029f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=91520e3b&sv=2)

Example - Speed Double Value

Typical game plays have an **unwritten rule** that helps keep consistency at all levels. That rule is simple: Speeds should always be **Double** or **Half** the tempo of the current BPM. You may also **Quadruple** or **One-fourt**h the speed as the game presents it with a double rabbit/snail

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F1OVSvXUL9phSazKyBpKu%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5243caa5-c128-4568-b459-ff480765ed3a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=22fa771c&sv=2)

Example - Double Tempo

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/bpm-speeds#greater-than-text-indication)

\-> Text Indication

Indicating in text format the speed is going to change in an inconsistent way, usually helps players get prepared ahead for an irregular gameplay style, making it a great way to stop surprises

# Scroll Screen | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/scroll-screen.md)
.

This event can stack multiple instances on the same tile

Video

Event Settings

Info

Event Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Scroll speed

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Set how fast your screen moves and loops around itself _Works on X and Y axis_

Angle offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Used to set the start delay of the event, in degrees

_(0º = on hit)_

Event tag

Text

Sets a tag that indentifies this event to other events. Can be used for repetition or easy event set-ups

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FdemTWc7J84DZXsaZNqsX%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29f6adc7-c693-42ca-a104-33c4047d5bb8&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e3f61d96&sv=2)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FWrt0iLDnBabHIFk1oPCg%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D220c081a-7a8e-4bbc-a129-b733213bfb4a&width=69&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8504493c&sv=2) -> Scroll Screen icon

. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/move-camera.md)
.

This event can stack multiple instances on the same tile

Video

Event Settings

Info

Event Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Duration

Numerical

The amount of beats the movement will last

Relative to

Multiple Selection

Set from each POV you want your camera to work with

Position

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Set the camera's new position _Works on X and Y axis_

Rotation

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Set the camera rotation angle

Zoom

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Set how far your camera moves from you

Angle offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Used to set the start delay of the event, in degrees

_(0º = on hit)_

Ease

Multiple Selection

Sets which easing is used for the transition animation of this event

Event tag

Text

Sets a tag that indentifies this event to other events. Can be used for repetition or easy event set-ups

_You can check all easing behavior on the_ _Event Skillful Formatting and Showcases -_ [_Easing Showcase_](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/easing-showcase)
 _section_

# Freeroam Segment | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/dlc-events/freeroam-segment.md)
.

This event cannot stack multiple instances on the same tile

Video

Event Settings

Info

Event Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Duration

Numerical

Amount of time in beats the freeroam section will last

Freeroam area size

Numerical

Area size of the freeroam section _determined by x and y values_

Position offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Sets the starting position of freeroam tiles compared to last tile _determined by x and y values_

Exit transition duration

Numerical

Amount of time in beats in which the exit ending transition will last

Ease

Multiple Selection

Sets which easing is used for the exit transition animation of this event

Hitsound for onbeats

Multiple Selection

Hitsound that will play for onbeats hits

Hitsound for offbeats

Multiple Selection

Hitsound that will play for offbeats hits

Countdown ticks

Numerical

Number of beats, counting timer for the regular tiles beat to start

Angle correction

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Changes the planets animation for the ending transition

_You can check all easing behavior on the_ _Event Skillful Formatting and Showcases -_ [_Easing Showcase_](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/easing-showcase)
 _section_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F02vqcfaQ1VUM1tXUgcau%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8ddcf1a9-0097-4444-8ddf-c83ef66f2dec&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=54f7e19f&sv=2)

Video

Event Settings

Info

Event Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Duration

Numerical

Amount of extra loops in the holds, representing extra hold time

Travel distance

Numerical

Distance between the hold starting tile and the hold ending tile

Landind animation

Radio Selection

Enables an animation of circle precision, synced to the ending of the hold

# Move Decorations | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/decoration-events/move-decorations.md)
.

This event can stack multiple instances on the same tile

Video

Event Settings

Info

Event Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Duration

Numerical

The amount of beats the decoration animation will last

Tag

Text

Sets a tag that indentifies this decoration to other events. _Can be used on events_

Image

Image File

Your decoration file. This serves in case you haven't applied any decor or tags to the event

Position offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

How offset the decor will place compared to the original event tile position. _Works on X and Y axis_

Pivot offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Alters the pivot of the decoration, changing its center point

Rotation offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

How much the decor will rotate, compared to its last rotation value

Scale

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Indicates which new size the decor will be

Color

Hex Code

Changes the base color of the decoration

Opacity

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Changes how transparent the decoration gets

Depth

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Place the decor on virtual layers of depth to create the illusion of distance

Parallax

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Changes the travel distance of the decor from the camera's POV.

Parallax offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Changes the starting position of the decor's travel distance from the camera's POV.

_Works on X and Y axis_

Angle offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Used to set the start delay of the event, in degrees _(0º = on hit)_

Ease

Multiple Selection

Sets which easing is used for the transition animation of this event

Event tag

Text

Sets a tag that indentifies this event to other events. Can be used for repetition or easy event set-ups

Mask Type

Multiple Selection

Use decorations as mask to remodel other decorations shape and colors

Use Mask depth

Radio Selection

Select if your mask occupies several depth layers when moving decorations

Mask Begin depth

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Indicates which layer the mask's depth effect starts

Mask End depth

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Indicates which layer the mask's depth effect ends

_You can check all easing behavior on the_ _Event Skillful Formatting and Showcases -_ [_Easing Showcase_](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/easing-showcase)
 _section_

_You can also check all masking behavior on the_ _Decoration and Text Creative Format -_ [_Masking Decorations_](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format/blending-and-masking)
 _section_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FNGXEuzPhIP3AdezBxzCw%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d0aab6b-26b2-4a05-a28e-97a199aa0d62&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2d331d70&sv=2)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FEYjJGC4oWFhYuZm7VTuo%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddf5a2518-668a-4b52-897c-cde73d7ab017&width=73&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=57c1dd98&sv=2) -> Move Decorations icon

**Purple Icons** can only be seen on the editing side. During gameplay, they disappear but work as the same

[PreviousDecoration Events](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/decoration-events)

# Image Decorations | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format/image-decorations.md)
.

Decoration Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Image

Image File

Your decoration file

Position

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Set the decoration's position _Works on X and Y axis_

Relative to

Multiple Selection

Set from each POV you want your decoration to work with

Pivot offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Alters the pivot of the decoration, changing its center point

Rotation

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Set the decoration rotation angle

Lock Rotation

Radio Selection

Select if you want your decor to rotate with your camera rotation

Scale

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Indicates which size the decoration will be

Lock Scale

Radio Selection

Select if you want your decor to scale with your camera zoom

Decoration Tiling

Numerical

Clones your decorations into smaller full images within the decor area _Works on X and Y axis_

Color

Hex Code

Changes the base color of the decoration

Opacity

Numerical

Changes how transparent the decoration gets

Depth

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Place the decor on virtual layers of depth to create the illusion of distance

Parallax

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Changes the travel distance of the decor from the camera's POV _Works on X and Y axis_

Parallax Offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Changes the starting position of the decor's travel distance from the camera's POV

_Works on X and Y axis_

Tag

Text

Sets a tag that indentifies this decoration. _Can be used on events_

Image Smoothing

Radio Selection

Select if you want your image digitally smoothed

Blend Mode

Multiple Selection

Blend decorations with each other and mix their colors

Mask Type

Multiple Selection

Use decorations as mask to remodel other decorations shape and colors

Fail Hitbox

Radio Selection

Select if your decoration acts as a fail mechanism when the planets hit the decoration's hitboxes

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FvKq5vBoCm3mS1J88UP7f%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f07f1a0-f66e-4494-afb0-763ed0db394f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ada25991&sv=2)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fx7nIlkpmzePSyJBvAEvO%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D09294f4c-26d1-4fd0-abde-6676cbde1ef2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aef89814&sv=2)

# Conditional Events Prep | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/conditional-events-prep.md)
.

This practice is related to [Set Conditional](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/event-modifiers/set-conditional-events)
 Events

Setting conditions for certain events to happen during the level, is a great to create diversified content for each gameplay input. Basically, we can indicate the game when and what to do in case something happens in the level according to the player's input.

Here is a good example of Conditional Events happening in the background of this level:

📝ADOFAI - XT-X Options, gameplay by Nichipe

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/conditional-events-prep#how-to-set-the-conditions-so-events-can-work)

How to set the conditions, so events can work?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

_Check the_ _Event Modifiers_ _-_ [_Set Conditional Events_](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/event-modifiers/set-conditional-events)
 _to properly initiate the event_

Every event, which includes an **Event tag** setting, is available to use on the Conditional Events. For starters, let's use Set Text and Move Decoration as example

Create a text using the Decorations Tab, let's leave the text empty for now. Next, add a new decoration and use any image you would like. Before we move into the actual events, we properly tag each decoration with their unique name

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FzjrKyYq2vQcFLcFcfIOQ%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9459d96-e591-4340-889a-aa2628ad4f6f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3869e216&sv=2)

Example - Text tag

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FyCTywB1mTCXQURNkfflR%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc1f5ba94-ddb8-47ae-8b2b-f15310f244b7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=34129cfa&sv=2)

Example - Image tag

Now, for our events, let's set a losing message and a decor rotation when the players lose during the level. Don't forget to add the previous tags into your events, so they work. We are also adding the Event tag to our tag, so the conditional event can find which events to use.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FnrQW2RJlMPmrpdS1ej8Z%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6f0a32e-b54d-47c6-b67c-204d09a06935&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bdd97c&sv=2)

Example - Move Decoration prep for conditional event

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F6V8Sk0ejBxDusE5NVlDc%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D19a54f67-3fa1-4ba2-8e0d-bfeb6bf678c0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d4cbc190&sv=2)

Example - Set Text prep for conditional event

Make sure, when using tags for Conditional Events, to use the **same event tag** on all your desired events, as each condition only accepts one tag.

Events will only work for Conditional Events if they are built on the same tile as the conditional event

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FVRs174SuJuKwlhrptv4j%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb907af7-da33-4810-8a3c-49d1b31e9f52&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8ad7a96a&sv=2)

Example - Event tag used for all "Loss" Events

All it's needed now is to add the same event tag, into the "Loss" condition tag, since we only want these events to activate when the player loses. Rest assured, these events won't play in normal conditions when everything is set for conditional purposes.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/level-preparation-and-assisting-techniques/good-practices/conditional-events-prep#multiple-conditions-set-at-the-same-time)

Multiple Conditions set at the same time


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Several events can be used for several conditions set at the same time, independently of what type they are. Let's use as an example several texts showing when the player input drifts from perfect using only one text decor.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FMZZCCFPe14Cu6naAeTpt%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc766144-cbd9-458c-94de-2e478d78a30b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7972c659&sv=2)

Example 2 - Setting a text for when the input is Too Early / Too Late with a unique event tag

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F0IMHYY3HjLSwrJfyLg1l%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46481066-da48-4ebf-8d69-15c573a61f91&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6e38eb0b&sv=2)

Example 2 - Setting a text for when the input is EPerfect/LPerfect with a unique event tag

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fspe6ei4QFJABIt7MAouR%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D74fadea3-4644-4e76-85b2-788ab654649b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eae0d8e1&sv=2)

Example 2 - Setting a text for when the input is Early/Late with a unique event tag

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Febtik3qAgC2XOCD878vr%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d465aef-ad98-4ea7-b622-72d1df704970&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=147bea53&sv=2)

Example 2 - Setting a text for when the input is Perfect with a unique event tag

For this example, we don't want any conditions for when the player loses, so we don't need to do any changes. For now, let's fill up the event tags in their respective places.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FTmQRMbcNSNeeIPEMeuSx%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd91b400f-0393-4563-9fcd-55f13518a23f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5912e5b&sv=2)

Example 2 - Setting each event tag on their respective condition

Everything should work properly now. All the event tags were placed, and all events were set and connected to their conditions!

# Set Filter | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/set-filter.md)
.

This event can stack multiple instances on the same tile

Video

Event Settings

Info

Event Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Filter

Multiple Selection

Set which filter you want your screen to apply

Set to

Radio Selection

Turn the selected filter on or off

Intensity

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Select how intense you want your filter to show _Some filters are absolute_

Duration

Numerical

Set for how long the filter takes to reach the desired settings

Ease

Multiple Selection

Sets which easing is used for the transition animation of this event

Disable others

Radio Selection

Select this if you need the active filters to switch off

Angle offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Used to set the start delay of the event, in degrees

_(0º = on hit)_

Event tag

Text

Sets a tag that indentifies this event to other events. Can be used for repetition or easy event set-ups

_You can check all easing behavior on the_ _Event Skillful Formatting and Showcases -_ [_Easing Showcase_](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/easing-showcase)
 _section_

_You can check all filters on the_ _Event Skillful Formatting and Showcases -_ [_Filters Showcase_](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/filters-showcase)
 _section_

Note that these do **NOT** showcase all possible interactions for each filter, but rather, a simple showcase of how each filter works, so feel free to experiment more when making levels

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FzVbSaG0UsdQz4KfKRysq%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57d1aedc-f312-4a04-8fba-0d9e184e3c24&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ef36a2e2&sv=2)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F3fdqgUjPsBmECMMjMcJY%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da13241b8-6cbe-4e88-b3fc-990433e183d9&width=74&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5224a7a3&sv=2) -> Set filter icon

**Purple Icons** can only be seen on the editing side. During gameplay, they disappear but work as the same

# Flash | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/flash.md)
.

This event can stack multiple instances on the same tile

Video

Event Settings

Info

**Might cause epilepsy WARNING**

Event Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Duration

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Set how long the flash will occur

Plane

Radio Selection

Selected if you want your flash to affect the entire screen or just the background

Start color

Hex Code

The event will start flashing with this color

Start opacity

Numerical

How transparent you want the starting color to show

End color

Hex Code

The event will end flashing with this color

End opacity

Numerical

How transparent you want the ending color to show

Angle offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Used to set the start delay of the event, in degrees

_(0º = on hit)_

Ease

Multiple Selection

Sets which easing is used for the transition animation of this event

Event tag

Text

Sets a tag that indentifies this event to other events. Can be used for repetition or easy event set-ups

_You can check all easing behavior on the_ _Tool Event Skillful Formatting and Showcases -_ [_Easing Showcase_](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/easing-showcase)
 _section_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FtnqhDWvlk9AZlvzTsOKN%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf7ed0e3-dbb8-4fe3-8c5d-386e35875d8f&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=66b6cafc&sv=2)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F7lhpe6UEjs6RjMiKo2Tr%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a74cc85-de80-4027-801b-777a2fd818da&width=75&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dabc0c05&sv=2) -> Flash icon

Be aware that the constant and bad use of this event might cause people to suffer epilepsy. Use it with **moderation**

**Purple Icons** can only be seen on the editing side. During gameplay, they disappear but work as the same

# Set Background | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/set-background.md)
.

This event can stack multiple instances on the same tile

Video

Event Settings

Info

Event Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Color

Hex Code

Sets a solid color for the background

Image

Image File

Your Background file

Image color

Hex Code

Changes the base color of the background image

Parallax

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Changes the travel distance of the background from the camera's POV.

Display mode

Multiple Selection

What looping your background will display in case the image reaches any of its edges

Image smoothing

Radio Selection

Select if you want yor image digitally smoothed

Lock rotation

Radio Selection

Locks the background from rotating with the camera

Loop background

Radio Selection

Locks the background from moving with the camera

Scaling ratio

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Indicates which size the background will be

Angle offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Used to set the start delay of the event, in degrees

_(0º = on hit)_

Event tag

Text

Sets a tag that indentifies this event to other events. Can be used for repetition or easy event set-ups

# Multi-presses | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/multi-presses.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/multi-presses#what-are-multi-presses)

What are multi-presses?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Multi-presses are tiles that involved you hitting multiple keys on your keyboard at the same time. (RIP one-button rhythm game). A good example of this gimmick being played is on the official world RJ, where the blue tiles represent two key presses into one tile.

📝World RJ - Fear Grows, video by Nichipe

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/general-gimmicks/multi-presses#how-to-create-a-multi-press-tile)

How to create a multi-press tile?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Let's start by indicating which tiles will represent our multi-press tiles. For this example, we are coloring the tiles with blue. But the format you choose for this gimmick is entirely up to you

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FqJbi6pRJdZCv604juL4c%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D00e519a2-3e19-44cf-84ba-a61077d0b086&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=74d85445&sv=2)

Editor - Multi Presses build

Click on the tile you want your multi-press to happen, you will notice a bubble for "custom angle" on the right corner. Click that.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FIYdeDIqYuXxjB8G61MkP%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9ec88ac5-3e5a-43ef-afec-1d814830d7a6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ec5380d6&sv=2)

Editor - Angle Input

Here, you have two options. A Bubble for regular tiles and one for mid-spin tiles. For this example, we will be using the mid-spin option. Let's insert the value 0.01 into the text box and click the mid-spin bubble.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FgL1kayBvL6xhnmYjnEyb%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D207b3f70-4b24-44f0-890f-62d3ffc7a849&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=18a92907&sv=2)

Editor - Insert value angle

A mid-spin tile will be created. 0.01º is the lowest angle possible inside the editor. But in beats, is 0.0000555555555556 of ONE beat. This is such a small value that we can not play it as a separate hit note, which makes the gimmick of two keys hit a reality for the game.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FP2JaRr7fVO3sPSXFwe8r%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6f88cbc9-a4f9-476e-a0cd-aa4b8b95d4e4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5f6b87ad&sv=2)

Editor - Mid Spin Add of 0.01º

Since we associated the color as our multi-press tile, let's use Position Track to hide the mid-spin note, turning its opacity to 0%

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FyYkvVeQXRDyXJJHp8j6F%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29eb6354-b112-4f65-a6dc-6488197a09e8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d8c02eb0&sv=2)

Editor - Position Track into 0 Opacity

Now you just repeat this process over all your desired tiles. Look how all the mid-spin tiles are set and hidden from the player's view now.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252Fxr5MIcnTySQKQUO4XyG6%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc262e1c9-506c-4769-aea5-2b69dd7b9069&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5a9d17cd&sv=2)

Editor - All mid-spins are set as multi-presses

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FepAEOHRLka3EHqYSZABD%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddcb5b52f-ba9a-44a2-aaa5-e69981d5f275&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9e1cab65&sv=2)

Editor - Multi-press hit validation

Congratulations, you have now created a multi-press level!

# Bloom | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/events/visual-effects/bloom.md)
.

This event can stack multiple instances on the same tile

Video

Event Settings

Info

Event Setting Name

Type Validation

Setting Description

Set to

Radio Selection

Set this event to on or off

Threshold

Numerical

Set the brightness level under the bloom

Intensity

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Set how strong the bloom effect will be

Color

Hex Code

Changes the base color of the bloom

Duration

Numerical

Set how many beats your bloom takes to reach desired settings

Ease

Multiple Selection

Sets which easing is used for the transition animation of this event

Angle offset

Numerical _Accepts both integers_

Used to set the start delay of the event, in degrees

_(0º = on hit)_

Event tag

Text

Sets a tag that indentifies this event to other events. Can be used for repetition or easy event set-ups

_You can check all easings behavior on the_ _Event Skillful Formatting and Showcases -_ [_Easing Showcase_](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/easing-showcase)
 _section_

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FBGHaHCOqDgWDjXujzasl%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29605893-d338-4bed-86a9-fee2bfb5da6f&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=397f6ac4&sv=2)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FXBhG0sckH8QmjvRrx42V%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6b4208cc-05fd-410d-b1fd-ceba00090529&width=73&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=46712e30&sv=2) -> Bloom icon

**Purple Icons** can only be seen on the editing side. During gameplay, they disappear but work as the same

# Blending And Masking | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format/blending-and-masking.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format/blending-and-masking#blend-descriptions)

Blend Descriptions


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Learn more about Blending on [Adobe Website](https://helpx.adobe.com/photoshop/using/blending-modes.html)

Blend Option

Description

Screen

Looks at each channel’s color information and multiplies the inverse of the blend and base colors.

Linear Dodge

Looks at the color information in each channel and brightens the base color to reflect the blend color by increasing the brightness.

Overlay

Multiplies or screens the colors, depending on the base color. Patterns or colors overlay the existing pixels while preserving the highlights and shadows of the base color.

Soft Light

Darkens or lightens the colors, depending on the blend color. The effect is similar to shining a diffused spotlight on the image.

Difference

Looks at the color information in each channel and subtracts either the blend color from the base color or the base color from the blend color, depending on which has the greater brightness value.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format/blending-and-masking#blending-mixes)

Blending Mixes


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Decorations have the same blending method, two layers of depth, (Red = Layer 1 ~ Blue = Layer 2) and no masking

### 

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format/blending-and-masking#no-blending)

Mask Descriptions


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mask Option

Description

Mask Other Decoration

Use this option to set a mask's shape and color to other decorations

Show Overlay

Use this option on the decoration you want the defined mask to be on top of

Hide Overlay

Use this option on the decoration you want the defined mask to be on removed of

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format/blending-and-masking#masking-mixes)

Masking Mixes


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All decorations have the same depth layer and no blending

# Color and Alpha Styling | ADOFAI EDITOR GUIDE

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format/color-and-alpha-styling.md)
.

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format/color-and-alpha-styling#understanding-hex-color-values)

Understanding Hex Color values


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252F7PP09WAA7OE4YV32L32W%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f8e80da-c44a-4b7b-ba91-9ba9e7a6b88b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=45dc3bda&sv=2)

Colors - UI Styling

Hexadecimal is similar to the decimal system (0 to 9) but instead of having 10 digits to count, hexadecimal has 16 (0 ~ 9, A, B, C, D, E, and F). To make it simple to understand, just imagine A being the next number after 9, which is A = 10. Do the same for the rest of the Hexadecimal letters.

Hexadecimal color range: FFCC8833

*   **Red:** First two hexadecimal digits of every number (FF000000)
    
*   **Green:** Second two hexadecimal digits of every number (00FF0000)
    
*   **Blue:** Third two hexadecimal digits of every number (0000FF00)
    
*   **Alpha:** Last two hexadecimal digits of every number (000000FF)
    

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F484108807-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fipb5NkFjq0eBOIGewqlQ%252Fuploads%252FQSqQM2abxrHWyinQOt8f%252Fimagem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45ca4d35-be77-4481-bc03-47ac942ccb29&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=66275d14&sv=2)

Colors - Hexadecimal color range distribution

Type Value

Description

Red

Indicates how much red the image has _00 = No red ,_ _FF = Full Red_

Green

Indicates how much green the image has _00 = No green ,_ _FF = Full Green_

Blue

Indicates how much blue the image has _00 = No blue,_ _FF = Full Blue_

Alpha

Indicates how opaque the image will be _00 = Transparent,_ _FF = Full Opaque_

_Just for mere curiosity, RGBA Colors (255, 255, 255, 255) values are the decimal way to display the 00~FF Hexadecimal values. Check more about numerical bases at_ [_this website_](https://www.eatyourbytes.com/decimal-binary-and-hexadecimal-numbers-from-0-to-255/)

[](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format/color-and-alpha-styling#color-value-listing)

Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/editor-menu-list/background-settings.md). # Background Settings ## List of Settings | Setting Name | Type Validation | Description | | :-------------------------------: | :----------------: | :----------------------------------------------------------------------------------: | | Background Color | Hex Code | Color range value for the background color | | Show Tutorial Background pattern | Radio Selection | Choose between showing the background pattern or not in your levels | | Tutorial Background pattern color | Hex Code | Color range value for the background pattern | | Tutorial Background shape | Multiple Selection | Remove or use different variants of the background shapes in your levels | | Tutorial Background shape color | Hex Code | Color range value for the background shapes | | Background Image | Image File | Image to act as the background | | Image Color | Hex Code | Color range value for the background image contrast | | Parallax | Numerical | Indicate both X & Y values to displace the background from the player's POV | | Display Mode | Multiple Selection | Select different forms of background placement | | Image Smoothing | Radio Selection | Indicate if you allow to smooth digitally the background of your level | | Lock Rotation | Radio Selection | Indicate if you allow the background to rotate with the camera | | Loop Background | Radio Selection | Indicate if you allow the background image to repeat itself to fill its outside area | | Scaling Ratio | Numerical | How much zoom, in %, the background will have |

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/YhdYM9SEk8K2mxH2ryQR)

Editor - Background Settings Tab

# Unknown

\> For the complete documentation index, see \[llms.txt\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt). Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset.md). # Finding the Correct BPM & Offset ## Understanding why using the correct Offset and BPM is important While making levels, we often find our songs to be quite difficult to work with because the bases for level creation aren't set automatically for us when adding the song file. This is because every level requires some \*\*preparation\*\* before the actual level editing occurs So, here is what you should do before anything else when adding your song file to the level: \* Find the \*\*correct BPM\*\* - \*beats per minute\* \* Find the \*\*correct Offset\*\* - \*how delayed the game starts compared to the song start\* ### How to find the ideal BPM for your song {% hint style="info" %} If possible, ask the artist who made the song for its BPM, which will save a considerable amount of time. {% endhint %} Unfortunately, the ADOFAI editor \*\*does not include\*\* any tools to help you find the song's BPM, so here are some external websites you can use instead: ### • BPM Finders

|     |     |     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Beatsperminuteonline** | _`Tapper`_ | [How to use](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset.md#beatsperminuteonline) | [https://www.beatsperminuteonline.com/](https://www.beatsperminuteonline.com/) | [/files/jbVYHGPumwQWgpnuSRK9](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/jbVYHGPumwQWgpnuSRK9) |
| **All8 Tap for Beats Per Minute** | _`Tapper`_ | [How to use](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset.md#all8-tap-for-beats-per-minute) | [https://www.all8.com/tools/bpm.htm](https://www.all8.com/tools/bpm.htm) | [/files/rUHAEg2rjFiIKxMlnrFy](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/rUHAEg2rjFiIKxMlnrFy) |
| **VocalRemover** | _`Tapper`_ | [How to use](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset.md#vocalremover-tap-tempo) | [https://vocalremover.org/key-bpm-finder](https://vocalremover.org/key-bpm-finder) | [/files/obk3ijVZwQayBcX78kbf](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/obk3ijVZwQayBcX78kbf) |
| **ArrowVortex** | _`AutoFinder`_ | [How to use](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset.md#arrowvortex) | [https://arrowvortex.ddrnl.com/](https://arrowvortex.ddrnl.com/) | [/files/kWZMTfSlhBe26NRm2MMU](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/kWZMTfSlhBe26NRm2MMU) |
|     |     |     |     |     |

\### How to find the correct offset for your level Unfortunately, the ADOFAI editor \*\*does not include\*\* any tools to help you find the song's offset, so here are some external tools you can use instead: ### • Offset Finders

|     |     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Audacity** | [How to use](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/finding-the-correct-bpm-and-offset.md#audacity) | [https://www.audacityteam.org/download/windows/](https://www.audacityteam.org/download/windows/) | [/files/M0UAAHmwK6hnWd9XeLME](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/M0UAAHmwK6hnWd9XeLME) |

{% hint style="info" %} You can always \*\*change\*\* the pitch down of your level, to test how accurate your BPM and offset are. Just remember to switch it back to 100% when you are done {% endhint %} {% hint style="warning" %} \*Both these methods are only as accurate as their user's precision. If you still have trouble finding either the Offset or the BPM, ask someone from the community to help. It's always great to have second opinions!\* {% endhint %} \*\*\* #### • beatsperminuteonline How to use: \*\*\\\[1\]\*\* After entering the website, it's important to \*\*play your song\*\* in the background, as this website will follow the \*\*user's input\*\* to the beat. \*\*\\\[2\]\*\* Press any key \*or your mouse on the BPM button\* and try to be consistent with your taps. This is where the bpm counter will present you with a number that should be your song's bpm. \*Try to do at least 40 consistent presses.\* \*\*\\\[3\]\*\* Use the value you acquired on the Song Settings - Beats per minute, and you are all ready!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/R1XU6ad3EJIg5DRtLRBh)

**\[1\]** Beatsperminuteonline Website

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/xP1zwutNjbNWntASz2vV)

**\[2\]** Beatsperminuteonline - BPM found

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/HFhqAJ1GMk2dpSdSxVH6)

**\[3\]** Game Editor, Song Settings - Correct BPM

\*\*\* #### •All8 Tap for Beats Per Minute II. How to use: \*\*\\\[1\]\*\* This one works in a very similar way to Beatsperminuteonline, however, it is more minimalistic and straight to the point. It's mostly a question of preference, so feel free to try both and see which suits you better. \*\*\\\[2\]\*\* Press any key \*or your mouse on the BPM button\* and try to be consistent with your taps. This is where the bpm counter will present you with a number that should be your song's bpm. \*Try to do at least 40 consistent presses.\* \*\*\\\[3\]\*\* Use the value you acquired on the Song Settings - Beats per minute, and you are all ready!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/HYnaggXrWWakdouMV1TO)

**\[1\]** All8 Tap for Beats Per Minute Website

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/rUHAEg2rjFiIKxMlnrFy)

**\[2\]** All8 Tap for Beats Per Minute - BPM found

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/ZQ4AwcNXqAmvrZveUmpb)

**\[3\]** Game Editor, Song Settings - Correct BPM

\*\*\* #### • VocalRemover Tap Tempo III. How to use: \*\*\\\[1\]\*\* VocalRemover has a BPM autofinder and a BPM tapper. Only the BPM tapper will be covered. \*\*\\\[2\]\*\* In the "\*Tap Tempo\*" function, is it required by the user to press space at least 20 times in the rhythm of the song to have the estimated BPM, but the user can do more if they want a more consistent result. This is more precise than the last two, but in exchange, requires a higher precision of the user to get an accurate estimation. \*\*\\\[3\]\*\* Use the value you acquired on the Song Settings - Beats per minute, and you are all ready!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/uJW8Irq827loyVsl3qR1)

**\[1\]** VocalRemover Website - Song Key and BPM Finder

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/obk3ijVZwQayBcX78kbf)

**\[2\]** BPM acquired after tapping on the rhythm

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/RIJu7juUFdLOOgayJW0r)

**\[3\]** Game Editor, Song Settings - Correct BPM

\*\*\* #### • ArrowVortex IV. How to use: \*\*\\\[1\]\*\* ArrowVortex is mainly a program made for making charts for 4k rhythm games, like StepMania, Osu!Mania, Quaver, Eterna, etc.; but it can actually be useful to find the BPM of songs for other games, like in this case, ADOFAI. \*\*\\\[2\]\*\* To download ArrowVortex, just simply use one of the download options provided by its website, and extract the .rar file.\\ When you open ArrowVortex, it should look like this. \*(Picture below)\* \*\*\\\[3\]\*\* To find the BPM of the song you will use, you are firstly to open the song file in the program. To do so, click the "\*File\*" button (I), then the "\*Open\*" button (II). After that, find the song file in your selected directory and open it. \*Press\* \`F3\` \*to hear beat ticks, that correspond with the current BPM.\* \*\*\\\[4\]\*\* After opening the song in the program, click on the "\*Tempo\*" button, then "\*Adjust sync\*". \*\*\\\[5\]\*\* This will bring you to the "\*ADJUST SYNC\*" settings, where the ArrowVoltex has a built-in feature to automatically find the BPM of a song, when pressing "\*Find BPM\*". \*If the BPM the autofinder gave was an rational number, the safest thing to do is \*\*use the nearest integer number\*\*.\* \*\*\\\[6\]\*\* After finding the BPM, put the value you acquired on the Song Settings - Beats per minute, and you are all ready!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/xxXfmvmoZ3D6B3Y5srTo)

**\[1\]** ArrowVortex Website

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/JIMkK0rXpMeZgvIIhsqu)

**\[2\]** ArrowVortex Main Menu

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/cEP170TY4FRMOIr2htgd)

**\[3\]** Order of buttons to press

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/kG3yBtckFCX6tjAaIiiR)

**\[4\]** Order of buttons to press

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/kWZMTfSlhBe26NRm2MMU)

**\[5\]** "_ADJUST SYNC_" Menu

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/JuV8GbTKJ5kz7ej4RC38)

**\[6\]**

\*\*\* #### • Audacity V. How to use: \*\*\\\[1\]\*\* To find an offset that works in the game, you have to take into consideration: \* Where do you want the gameplay to start? When the music starts, or at a later point in the song? \*\*\\\[2\]\*\* To \*\*add a song\*\*, simply draw any audio file into the program, and a screen with the track's audio waves should appear. \*\*\\\[3\]\*\* If you notice any gap between the start and the blue waves, that means your song has offset. To find out, click on the top of the gap and use the \*\*Zoom + tool\*\* to take a closer look. \*\*\\\[4\]\*\* Finally, use your \*\*key arrows,\*\* or \*\*mouse click\*\* to place as close as possible, to the first blue high wave, to find a close-to-perfect offset from the \*\*start\*\* of your song. This value will match the start of your gameplay level (\*make sure to copy the time that is in milliseconds\*), use that value on the Song Settings - Offset, and you are all ready!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/NacVBepfoiI5R3JhdgP6)

**\[1\]** Audacity - Main Screen

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/7BgkDH5jBZ1raNKjzHuW)

**\[2\]** Audacity - Track display

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/QX0xdx7gv4BCq7M1F954)

**\[3\]** Audacity - Offset gap close up

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/acOhjnGZCESpHz14ZR6A)

**\[4\]** Audacity - Ideal game offset

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/pqKw0clBTb44tPLAEUph)

**\[5\]** Game Editor, Song Settings - Ideal Offset

# Unknown

\> For the complete documentation index, see \[llms.txt\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt). Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/workshop-and-level-hunting.md). # Workshop and Level Hunting ## Access the game's Steam Workshop Steam Workshop has vast other game content available for players to subscribe to and play as they like. To access the ADOFAI's workshop, head over to your game section on your Steam library and press Workshop

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/LWpmyFbuSfVEr2HZdhHp)

Steam Library - Game Tab

The game's workshop is now open. From Discussions, Screenshots, Videos, Guides, and much more, every piece of content can be found here, including all levels made by other players

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/0Uclcv2ElmMdfbajcRiA)

Steam - ADOFAI workshop

\## Finding new levels ### • By name To search for a specific artist, song, or level creator, write their name into the workshop search bar. All level content that matches your description, should appear right under

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/pvLQq0SuZEQnzX3GiUue)

Workshop - Search Bar

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/DJcrOrE3az0w4VlGGxen)

Workshop - Search Results

\### • By most recent uploaded Searching for new uploaded levels is simple. Under the search bar, there is a section for popular workshop tabs such as Most Popular, Last Updated, etc. In there, click the "Most Recent" to head over to the most recent uploaded levels section  

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/OrKVoflo6ppNNRrnScjZ)

Workshop - Browse Recent Items by Tag

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/C8EmAp9BkkVg6PWhiQws)

Workshop - Most Recent Levels

\### • By most popular As you open the game's workshop, you will be presented with the Top 9 most Popular levels of the week

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/cjsuh8danfIZms6Ckaa7)

Workshop - Top 9 Most Popular Levels of the week

To continue, you can press the "Most Popular Items" on the top of this area, or click under the search bar where it says "Most Popular"

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/yHFGXdqBG1T6D5mv8daa)

Workshop - Browse Popular Items by Tag

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/7KxVuEpsTr1GJLxCwgpm)

Workshop - Most Popular Levels of the week

In case you want to extend the period of time on the popular search, click on "Over time period" and select your search criteria

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/XRYKHiJmfpg2ptjgyxhP)

Workshop - Over Time Period List

\### • By Difficulty and Content available Levels can be searched by a difficult setting (steam evaluation, not gems) and/or their content available inside each level. Pressing any of the available options will direct you to the levels that meet the same criteria

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/cVG1OmGEMFZLCaGjH4HG)

Workshop - Browse by Difficulty / Content

{% hint style="info" %} Each setting will use the most popular of the week as the second criteria on finding levels with a selected Difficulty and/or Content {% endhint %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/go9LnYCvU3tdkLqODGOK)

Workshop - Browse by Content

\## Access your level files on the Workshop Your released levels can be found on the workshop inside the files you have posted. Just click "Your files" and then "Files you've posted"

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/BctF7BTuNrjRB3zQPufl)

Workshop - Files you've posted

A screen with all your published levels should appear!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/GPMNJfCyC01n0Jbsua0u)

Workshop - Your levels

\## Level Management On this page, right next to the subscribe button, you have owner controls, where you can make a series of changes to the display and collaboration of your levels

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/UmydK0gj8wAz7jASTQ4z)

Workshop - Level Editing Page

\### • Edit Title & Description Change the title and the file description of your level on the Steam Workshop

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/xmeBhGWDyKWYTp0fmVSG)

Workshop Owner Controls - Edit Tile & Description

{% hint style="warning" %} This will not change the in-game Artist/Song content or its level description. Merely changes the steam level display {% endhint %} ### • Add/edit images & videos In case you would like to attach the gameplay of your level and a few images to the level display, simply upload the image files here. In case your video is already on YouTube, feel free to add the URL to the YouTube Attachment

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/VOGldZwwAWE2qMruIh6G)

Workshop Owner Controls - Add / Edit Images & Videos

To manage your existing images & videos, click on the "X" simply to remove them. You can also drag them around to order them as you like

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/8ht8gEn7tIOWbjduqlD7)

Workshop Owner Controls - Manage Images & Videos

\### • Add/Remove Contributors If your level was made with more than one player, it's always great to give them credit too! Steam allows you to add and remove contributors from your friends list to your level

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/hXAlrSSEUDoH47WdmLz3)

Workshop Owner Controls - Manage Contributors

\### • Edit profile links In case you want to include any of your page & social media info into your levels, you can add them to your owner profile

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/2f0RSe2P6p1U7jV3yZkK)

Workshop Owner Controls - Level Creator links

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/PsgLJ4s4r5brm7XNqB3m)

Workshop Level - Contributors and Links

# Unknown

\> For the complete documentation index, see \[llms.txt\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt). Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/name-and-save-levels.md). # Name and Save Levels ## • Naming Rules ### ‣ General rules for level naming Naming your level is quite easy, although there are some \*\*precautions\*\* to take to ensure full compatibility across every OS version of the game. \* Levels \*\*can\*\* contain letters (a-z), numbers (0-9), dashes (-), underscore (\\\_), and periods (.); \* Levels permit these characters, but it is strongly advised to avoid using ampersands (&), equal signs (=), apostrophes ('), plus signs (+), commas (,), angle brackets (<,>), spaces ( ), consecutive periods (..), or any non-alphabetical symbols.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/XEhaRT9Ge1rMOewNFjgw)

Explorer - Good example of naming

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/S6kOYpMs52nSD13QJ72S)

Explorer - Bad example of naming

\*\*\* ### ‣ Naming levels to include tutorials When publishing levels, the workshop allows you to add tutorials to your levels. This is possible by including one file for each tutorial, grouping them with the \*LevelNameTutorialNumber.adofai\* format {% hint style="warning" %} \*\*Levelname\*\* must match your main file's name, so the game can associate the level with its tutorials, e.g., fragor1.adofai {% endhint %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/BX2vzpOZVw0Dvxc7h9b9)

Game Editor - Tutorial levels info

\*\*\* ## • Saving Levels ### ‣ Saving current Level

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/KZrIQPSKm8ALpNUgawts)

Editor Screen

When opening the editor, it is best to first \*\*save your level\*\* to create the necessary files from the very start. When saving, two files will be \*\*stored\*\* in your desired storage location: \* main.adofai \* backup.adofai {% hint style="info" %} The .adofai file format is used to save all of your levels. {% endhint %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/LVutTVNZJqKhw0UefV5V)

Editor - Top Menu Bar

To save your files, use your \*\*mouse\*\* to click on the \*\*Top Menu Bar\*\* where the :floppy\\\_disk: icon is. A drop-down list should appear with several options. For this part, we are focusing only on the \*\*Save\*\* and \*\*Save As...\*\* options.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/h5tU8qmHVokfOpfwz6yb)

Editor - Top Menu Bar opened

Regarding the \*\*Save\*\* option, it saves your current level progress. You can do this at any time after making changes to the level you are currently editing. {% hint style="info" %} You can also use \`Ctrl + S\` to save your current level. {% endhint %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/CoYrHGCsKb2Nm8ElekK6)

Editor - Top Menu Bar showing the level with a saved name

{% hint style="warning" %} When \*\*saving\*\* for the \*\*first time\*\*, your OS will request to save your file on your default directory. Make sure to select your desired location before confirming the first save. {% endhint %} \*\*\* ### ‣ Saving a new copy of the current Level [](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/name-and-save-levels.md#saving-a-new-copy-of-the-current-level)
The \*\*Save As...\*\* option creates a new file, unlike the \*\*Save\*\* option, which only updates the file you are currently working on. When you select this option, a new window appears. You can use the explorer tools on your computer to choose where to save your level and to properly name your file. {% hint style="info" %} All your decor, videos and files will be automatically storage on the new level location. {% endhint %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/e3wKlOKfXRGhKLyF4gDp)

Windows Explorer - Saving

{% hint style="info" %} You can also use \`Ctrl + Shift + S\` to save your level into a new file. {% endhint %} {% hint style="warning" %} Remember to include all the files, such as decorations and song audio files, when exporting levels onto .zip files. {% endhint %} \*\*\* --- # Agent Instructions This documentation is published with GitBook. GitBook is the documentation platform designed so that both humans and AI agents can read, navigate, and reason over technical content effectively. # Unknown

\> For the complete documentation index, see \[llms.txt\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt). Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement.md). # Tile Placement When it comes to constructing your level, the editor allows you to input each tile using the keyboard. There are also several methods to custom input an angle into the game. Before we continue, here is how the image will be subtitled for your understanding: \* \*\*White Letters\*\* - Keyboard Shortcut for tile placement \* \*\*Yellow Lines and Angles\*\* - 90º Separation placement and their associated angles \* \*\*Blue Lines and Angles\*\* - 45º Separation placement and their associated angles \* \*\*Green Lines and Angles\*\* - 30º Separation placement and their associated angles \* Red Lines and Angles - 15º Separation placement and their associated angles Let's now learn how to start counting angles \*\*according to the planet's rotation\*\*. All examples will be based out of a \`4/4\` Tempo Signature, which is the most commonly used around most songs. Each angle will be counting from 0º at its most right side radius, turning counter-clockwise and increasing this number until one full lap around is complete, where it goes back to 0º {% hint style="info" %} Learning this angle measure is efficient as your level will register angles into your Angle Data portion on your level files. Learn more about this on \[Surgery\](/english/surgery.md) Page {% endhint %} ## 90º Angles Starting from the basics, 90º placements are the simplest to use, as they represent our on-beats and off-beats of the song So let's consider that every time we hit 0º, we are doing 1 beat into the song beat

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/SImpohl7ggox8Ru8TiNH)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet where each sheet beat, equals the start of an angle (0º degrees)

\#### • Example 1 According to the game tile values, each tile represents an angle. Said angle is always base out of a counter-clockwise rotation from each beat, meaning 1 beat equals a starting point of an angle value. {% embed url="" %} With this in mind, every time you place a tile that isn't at beat start, its angle value will increase depending on how its angle ends, based from the beat start position.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/r8u3UAKCtOOMo3KO0Lkm)

Angle Rotation - 90º Splits

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/X06sxr6dOiwu1hIUAT7O)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, now with off-beat indicators

These vertical angles (90º and 270º) are what we call off-beats, meaning they can occur in between each beat #### • Example 2 Notice how the last horizontal tile had an angle of 180º? This is due to the origin point of the track being left to right, meaning this angle has a value of half a circle = 180º {% embed url="" %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/iBOVTEPKhf1wTtHagj9I)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, using off-beats

\#### • Example 3 Same logic applies here, each angle doing down has to turn a radius angle from the right to left, so 1 and a half circle = 270º {% embed url="" %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/ArbT9Yg2wSvtfUihK43Q)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, using long off-beats

\#### • Example 4 This case is a bit tricky. Each angle, compared to the last one, is a 90º different, however, when counting angles always remember to do it counter-clockwise, always starting from the beat line radius angle. {% embed url="" %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/FKOxRZVFFeqPhnr2X35X)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, mixing on-beats and off-beats

In conclusion, the angles presented in the square are 0º, 90º, 180º, 270º and 0º again. These are the angles the game file will record to make the square form. ## 45º Angles Now that we got the hang of on-beats and off-beats, let's add one more beat in between those. We now can play 4 beats inside each sheet beat. Each beat now is considered a sixteenth note

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/u2W2MDQybMWw0RwDSuaK)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet with 4 splits of 45º each sheet beat

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/nTENXBStGHhoLZBN3B74)

Angle Rotation - 45º Splits

\#### • Example 1 For this example, you can see that we created a tile that doesn't go fully horizontal, nor vertical. Sixteenths splitting allow notes to be played in between on-beats and off-beats {% embed url="" %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/U9H1TWZsUNBYblXsOWkm)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, showing 45º angles

\#### • Example 2 This is how a curve using the previous sixteenths angles would look like. As the sum of some sixteenths angles is equal to some off-beat and on-beat notes, those tiles also appear in the sixteenth curve to support the rhythm {% embed url="" %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/k7y059nQxHNwcLkFMVxG)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, curve tile using 45º angles

\#### • Example 3 Following the logic of a square pattern, we can build one using only intervals from the sixteenth placement, making all angles be hit in between on-beats and off-beats {% embed url="" %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/8L2IhNonbhP6FdkTFUod)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, making squares of sixteenth

\## 30º Angles These angles are mostly used for swing style of music, but the tile placement logic is the same. Take in consideration the 45º angles, where we placed 1 beat in between each on-beat and off-beat. This time, we are placing two beats in between each, rather than one, allowing us to count 24 beats in each sheet compared to the 16 beats from the 45º angles.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/nU0WyQ6KMDaTLEtmbKe5)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet with 6 splits of 30º each sheet beat

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/T1qfJSEjyTuD7EZsvsQT)

Angle Rotation - 30º Splits

{% hint style="info" %} You can access these shortcut tiles by holding \`Shift\` during the placement {% endhint %} #### • Example 1 Similar to 45º angle example, you can see that we created a tile that doesn't go fully horizontal, nor vertical, however since we have two beats between those angles, we can go beyond a perfect middle angle, but one that equally divided more to the horizontal angle, and another more to the vertical angle. {% embed url="" %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/j0bUAoUKGt7by2rqJQh2)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, showing 30º angles

\#### • Example 2 A curve that fits the 4/4 tempo is only possible if we use angles above 90º, which means 30º angles will be taking too long, requiring more than one sheet of 4/4 tempo. So we are using what we call the Hexagons (Curves made out of 120º angles). For this example, you can see how a swing beat can interact with a full rotation angle tile. {% embed url="" %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/4At6o5oPuetinJvQ1fYc)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, curve half hexagon using 60º angles

\#### • Example 3 Making squares on swing tempos can be a bit tricky. These come from a mix of on-beats and swings beats, to create the jazzy gameplay style. {% embed url="" %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/LauXwmgACpzuyZOLMtgD)

Tempo - 4/4 Sheet, making squares of 60º angles

Take into consideration that we are using the same angles for both the on-beats used, but alternatives to these angles are possible too. So get creative and place some tiles around, get creating! ## 15º Angles As an extra demonstration, the game allows you to fast input 15º Angles {% hint style="info" %} You can access these shortcut tiles by holding \`Shift\`\`+\`\` \`\`\` \` \`\` during the placement {% endhint %}

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/oQDZPhktps14n8s4JHN9)

Angle Rotation - 15º Splits

\## Custom Angles If any of these methods won't do for your levels, you can customize the exact angle you're looking for. To insert a custom angle, press the angle button after selecting the tile you want to insert the angle from.

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/Z7C7y6A9FtcpusGnG40n)

Editor - Insert Angle Button

From there, your options should look like the image below. Simply write your angle inside the text box, and click in one of the two tile types, to add the desired angle. (Regular tile or Mid-spin tile)

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/nc6cGLnBxZblUVkvr4Ke)

Editor - Select type of tile and angle text box

As you can see from the image below, one 15º angle tile was added to your track. This angle was the calculation from the last tile position angle + your angle value, creating a 165º angle that is a \*\*difference of 15º angle\*\*, between your last tile and the new one!

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/LI1yd0iYHghEMlJOVrMo)

Editor - Inserted a tile with 15º Angle apart, based on the last tile angle. (165º on the editor file)

{% hint style="warning" %} These angle inputs always measure clockwise from the \*\*last tile angle position\*\*, rather than angle 0º as explained for your Angle Data storage values. These inputs are merely informative to help place custom angles and their values are not stored based on them. {% endhint %} ## Tile Placement Shortcuts #### • 45º Angles

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/VXwgTDjjrhgrK0vOtYOX)

Shortcuts for 45º Angles tiles

\#### • 30º Angles

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/Yw81sIADROqh3KSqAgwf)

Shortcuts for 30º Angles tiles

\#### • \*\*15º Angles\*\*

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/xY15F3y94zIlVfLOwbR1)

Shortcuts for 15º Angles tiles

# Unknown

\> For the complete documentation index, see \[llms.txt\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/llms.txt). Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/english/surgery.md). # Surgery {% hint style="danger" %} Surgery can break your level in ways that are not recoverable! Please, if you are doing this, make sure to create a copy of your level before continuing {% endhint %} ## What is File Surgery? \*\*Surgery\*\* is the act of changing your level from writing directly into the file, rather than using the editor interface. As you know, whenever you save a level inside the Game Editor, a file that contains all the settings, actions, and decorations is updated. But in this case, we can do those changes over the file itself. ## What do I need to start the Surgery? -> A \*\*Text Editor\*\* software to read and edit the text file Here are a few you can use for free: \\---> Windows Notepad \*(You most likely already have this)\*\\ \\---> \[Notepad++\](https://notepad-plus-plus.org/downloads/) \*(Better Notepad)\*\\ \\---> Any IDE software \*(Integrated development environment)\* ## How to start Surgery on files.adofai? First, find the location of your file. You can easily open your most recent file with the \[Open the directory location window of most recent level\](/english/shortcuts-listing/editor-workflow/open-the-directory-location-window-of-most-recent-level.md) \*\*Shortcut\*\* After that, \`Mouse right-click\` on top of your level and click on \*\*Open with\*\* and select your Text Editor of choice. For this example, we will be using Notepad++

![](https://adofaieditor.gitbook.io/files/ppdhvVHuucwlYL5daNwF)

Notepad++ - Adofai Level Surgery Content

From here, it's a matter of adding and replacing values within each setting. Do have in mind, although you can put anything inside each setting, the game might not allow you to use them when you save and open the level file again ## Surgery Details \* \*\*Angle Data\*\* - Every tile angle will be storage here {% hint style="info" %} Check how to associate every tile angle on the \[Tile Placement\](/english/know-the-basics/tile-placement.md) section {% endhint %} \* \*\*Settings\*\* - All the information about the level, descriptions and starting values of events {% hint style="info" %} Check how to associate every level setting on the \[Editor Menu List\](/english/editor-menu-list.md) section {% endhint %} \* \*\*Actions\*\* - Every event added to the tiles will be set up here, including all its value settings {% hint style="info" %} Check how to associate every action with events in the \[Events\](/english/events.md) section {% endhint %} \* \*\*Decorations\*\* - Every decoration and text added will be saved here, including all its value settings {% hint style="info" %} Check how to associate every decoration on the \[Decoration and Text Creative Format\](/english/event-skillful-formatting-and-showcases/decoration-and-text-creative-format.md) section {% endhint %} ## Surgery advantages ### Easy Copy-Paste {% embed url="" %} ### Events at Tile 0 {% embed url="" %} --- # Agent Instructions This documentation is published with GitBook. GitBook is the documentation platform designed so that both humans and AI agents can read, navigate, and reason over technical content effectively.
